310: DroneScanner::~DroneScanner() {
311:     stop_scanning();
312:     cleanup_database_and_scanner();
313:     // Note: ChibiOS mutexes are automatically cleaned up with the object.
314:     // No explicit deinitialization needed - mutex is part of thread context.
315: }
316: 
317: void DroneScanner::initialize_wideband_scanning() {
318:     wideband_scan_data_.reset();
319:     setup_wideband_range(WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MIN, WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MAX);
320: }
321: 
322: void DroneScanner::setup_wideband_range(Frequency min_freq, Frequency max_freq) {
323:     // Use unified frequency limits from DroneConstants
324:     Frequency safe_min = std::max(min_freq, DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ);
325:     Frequency safe_max = std::min(max_freq, DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ);
326: 
327:     // Ensure min < max and apply hardware constraints
328:     if (safe_min >= safe_max) {
329:         safe_min = DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ;
330:         safe_max = DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ;
331:     }
332: 
333:     wideband_scan_data_.min_freq = safe_min;
334:     wideband_scan_data_.max_freq = safe_max;
335: 
336:     Frequency scanning_range = safe_max - safe_min;
337:     if (scanning_range > static_cast<Frequency>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz)) {
338:         // Check for integer overflow before calculating slices
339:         // Use int64_t to match rf::Frequency type and avoid sign comparison warning
340:         int64_t range_plus_width = static_cast<int64_t>(scanning_range) + static_cast<int64_t>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz);
341:         if (range_plus_width < scanning_range) {
342:             // Overflow detected - handle gracefully with single slice
343:             wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = 1;
344:         } else {
345:             wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = (static_cast<uint64_t>(range_plus_width) - 1) / settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz;
346:         }
347: 
348:         if (wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb > WIDEBAND_MAX_SLICES) {
349:             wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = WIDEBAND_MAX_SLICES;
350:         }
351:         // DIAMOND FIX: Cast to uint64_t before multiplication to prevent overflow
352:         // If slices_nb=50 and width=28MHz, result=1400MHz which overflows uint32_t Frequency
353:         Frequency slices_span = static_cast<Frequency>(static_cast<uint64_t>(wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb) * static_cast<uint64_t>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz));
354:         Frequency offset = ((scanning_range - slices_span) / 2) + (settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz / 2);
355:         Frequency center_frequency = safe_min + offset;
356: 
357:         std::generate_n(wideband_scan_data_.slices,
358:                        wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb,
359:                        [&center_frequency, slice_index = 0, this]() mutable -> WidebandSlice {
360:                            WidebandSlice slice;
361:                            slice.center_frequency = center_frequency;
362:                            slice.index = slice_index++;
363:                            center_frequency += settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz;
364:                            return slice;
365:                        });
366:     } else {
367:         wideband_scan_data_.slices[0].center_frequency = (safe_max + safe_min) / 2;
368:         wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = 1;
369:     }
370:     wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter = 0;
371: }
372: 
373: void DroneScanner::start_scanning() {
374:     if (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
375: 
376:     scanning_active_.store(true, std::memory_order_release);
377:     scan_cycles_ = 0;
378:     total_detections_ = 0;
379: }
380: 
381: void DroneScanner::stop_scanning() {
382:     if (!scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
383: 
384:     scanning_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
385: 
386:     // Wait for scanning thread to complete
387:     if (scanning_thread_ != nullptr) {
388:         chThdWait(scanning_thread_);
389:         scanning_thread_ = nullptr;
390:     }
391: 
392:     remove_stale_drones();
393: }
394: 
395: bool DroneScanner::load_frequency_database() {
396:     current_db_index_ = 0;
397: 
398:     freqman_load_options options;
399:     options.max_entries = 150;
400:     options.load_freqs = true;
401:     options.load_ranges = true;
402:     options.load_hamradios = true;
403:     options.load_repeaters = true;
404: 
405:     if (!freq_db_ptr_) return false;
406: 
407:     auto db_path = get_freqman_path("DRONES");
408:     bool sd_loaded = freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path);
409: 
410:     {
411:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
412: 
413:         if (!sd_loaded || freq_db_ptr_->empty()) {
414:             freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path, true);
415: 
416:             for (const auto& item : BUILTIN_DRONE_DB) {
417:                 freqman_entry entry{};
418:                 entry.frequency_a = item.freq;
419:                 entry.description = item.desc;
420:                 entry.type = freqman_type::Single;
421:                 entry.modulation = freqman_invalid_index;
422:                 entry.bandwidth = freqman_invalid_index;
423:                 entry.step = freqman_invalid_index;
424:                 entry.tone = freqman_invalid_index;
425:                 freq_db_ptr_->append_entry(entry);
426:             }
427: 
428:             sync_database();
429: 
430:             sd_loaded = !freq_db_ptr_->empty();
431:         }
432:     }
433: 
434:     if (freq_db_ptr_->entry_count() > 100) {
435:         handle_scan_error("Large database loaded");
436:     }
437: 
438:     freq_db_loaded_ = true;
439:     return !freq_db_ptr_->empty();
440: }
441: 
442: size_t DroneScanner::get_database_size() const {
443:     return freq_db_ptr_->entry_count();
444: }
445: 
446: void DroneScanner::set_scanning_mode(ScanningMode mode) {
447:     scanning_mode_ = mode;
448:     stop_scanning();
449:     reset_scan_cycles();
450: 
451:     if (scanning_mode_ == ScanningMode::DATABASE || scanning_mode_ == ScanningMode::HYBRID) {
452:         load_frequency_database();
453:     }
454: }
455: 
456: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup вместо switch для scanning_mode_name()
457: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
458: // Экономит ~40 байт Flash
459: const char* DroneScanner::scanning_mode_name() const {
460:     uint8_t idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(scanning_mode_);
461:     return (idx < 3) ? SCANNING_MODE_NAMES[idx] : "Unknown";
462: }
463: 
464: void DroneScanner::perform_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
465:     if (!scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
466: 
467:     // ?? ENHANCED: Adaptive timing with golden mean between speed and accuracy
468:     // Considering Cortex M4 limitations on Portapack (limited RAM, CPU)
469:     using namespace DroneConstants;
470:     uint32_t base_interval = DEFAULT_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS; // Base interval in milliseconds
471:     uint32_t adaptive_interval = base_interval;
472: 
473:     // Get current scan context
474:     size_t current_detections = get_total_detections();
475:     ThreatLevel max_threat = get_max_detected_threat();
476:     size_t tracked_count = tracked_count_;
477: 
478:     // ADAPTIVE STRATEGY:
479:     // - CRITICAL threats: scan fastest (250ms)
480:     // - HIGH threats: scan fast (400ms)
481:     // - MEDIUM threats: scan normal (750ms)
482:     // - LOW threats: scan slower (1000ms)
483:     // - NO threats: scan progressively slower (up to 2000ms)
484:     // - Balance: faster scanning of known drone bands, slower for empty bands
485: 
486:     if (max_threat >= ThreatLevel::CRITICAL) {
487:         // Critical threat detected - maximum speed scanning
488:         adaptive_interval = FAST_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS; // Fastest possible scan
489:     } else if (max_threat == ThreatLevel::HIGH) {
490:         // High threat - fast scanning
491:         adaptive_interval = 400;
492:     } else if (max_threat == ThreatLevel::MEDIUM) {
493:         // Medium threat - normal scanning
494:         adaptive_interval = NORMAL_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS;
495:     } else if (current_detections > 0 && tracked_count > 0) {
496:         // Have detections but low threat - maintain medium pace
497:         adaptive_interval = SLOW_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS;
498:     } else if (current_detections == 0 && scan_cycles_ > 10) {
499:         // No detections for a while - progressively slow down
500:         // Progressive slowdown: 1000ms  1500ms  2000ms (cap)
501:         uint32_t slowdown_multiplier = std::min(scan_cycles_ / 10, static_cast<uint32_t>(3));
502:         adaptive_interval = std::min(VERY_SLOW_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS, base_interval * slowdown_multiplier);
503:     }
504: 
505:     // Additional adjustment based on detection density
506:     if (current_detections > 5) {
507:         // Very high detection rate - maintain fast pace
508:         adaptive_interval = std::min(adaptive_interval, static_cast<uint32_t>(500));
509:     }
510:     
511:     // Apply adaptive interval
512:     chThdSleepMilliseconds(adaptive_interval);
513: 
514:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup вместо switch для perform_scan_cycle()
515:     // Scott Meyers Item 36: Never redefine an inherited non-virtual function
516:     // Экономит ~80 байт Flash, использует сырые указатели на методы (не std::function!)
517:     // Apply mode-specific adjustments
518:     uint8_t mode_idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(scanning_mode_);
519:     if (mode_idx < 3) {
520:         // Используем классный LUT DroneScanner::SCAN_FUNCTIONS для доступа к private методам
521:         (this->*DroneScanner::SCAN_FUNCTIONS[mode_idx])(hardware);  // Вызов метода через указатель
522:     }
523: 
524:     scan_cycles_++;
525: 
526:     // Adaptive sleep based on current situation
527:     if (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
528:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(adaptive_interval);
529:     }
530: }
531: 
532: void DroneScanner::perform_database_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
533:     size_t total_entries = 0;
534: 
535:     {
536:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
537:         if (!freq_db_ptr_ || freq_db_ptr_->empty()) {
538:             if (scan_cycles_ % 50 == 0) {
539:                 handle_scan_error("Database is empty");
540:             }
541:             return;
542:         }
543:         total_entries = freq_db_ptr_->entry_count();
544:     }
545: 
546:     const size_t batch_size = std::min(static_cast<size_t>(10), total_entries);
547: 
548:     // FIX: Use stack-allocated array instead of heap-allocated vector
549:     std::array<freqman_entry, 10> entries_to_scan{};
550:     size_t entries_count = 0;
551: 
552:     {
553:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
554:         if (freq_db_ptr_) {
555:             size_t db_entry_count = freq_db_ptr_->entry_count();
556:             if (db_entry_count > 0) {
557:                 for (size_t i = 0; i < batch_size; ++i) {
558:                     size_t idx = (current_db_index_ + i) % db_entry_count;
559:                     if (idx < db_entry_count && entries_count < entries_to_scan.size()) {
560:                         entries_to_scan[entries_count++] = (*freq_db_ptr_)[idx];
561:                     }
562:                 }
563:                 current_db_index_ = (current_db_index_ + batch_size) % db_entry_count;
564:             }
565:         }
566:     }
567: 
568:     for (size_t i = 0; i < entries_count; ++i) {
569:         const auto& entry = entries_to_scan[i];
570: 
571:         // CRITICAL: Check scanning flag EVERY iteration for immediate stop
572:         if (!scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
573: 
574:         Frequency target_freq_hz = entry.frequency_a;
575: 
576:         // CRITICAL: Enhanced frequency validation with overflow protection
577:         // Use unified frequency limits from DroneConstants
578:         const Frequency MIN_VALID_FREQ = DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ;
579:         const Frequency MAX_VALID_FREQ = DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ;
580: 
581:         // Validate frequency range
582:         if (target_freq_hz < MIN_VALID_FREQ || target_freq_hz > MAX_VALID_FREQ) {
583:             continue;
584:         }
585: 
586:         // Overflow protection check
587:         if (static_cast<uint64_t>(target_freq_hz) + 1000000ULL < static_cast<uint64_t>(target_freq_hz)) {
588:             continue;
589:         }
590: 
591:         // CRITICAL: Hardware tuning with proper validation
592:         if (hardware.tune_to_frequency(target_freq_hz)) {
593:             // Wait for PLL stabilization - broken into small chunks for responsiveness
594:             for(int w = 0; w < 3; w++) {
595:                 if(!scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
596:                 chThdSleepMilliseconds(10);
597:             }
598: 
599:             hardware.clear_rssi_flag();
600: 
601:             // Wait for fresh data with ABSOLUTE TIMEOUT (prevents infinite loop)
602:             constexpr systime_t RSSI_TIMEOUT_MS = 60;
603:             systime_t deadline = chTimeNow() + MS2ST(RSSI_TIMEOUT_MS);
604:             bool signal_captured = false;
605: 
606:             while (chTimeNow() < deadline) {
607:                 chThdSleepMilliseconds(5);
608:                 if (hardware.is_rssi_fresh()) {
609:                     signal_captured = true;
610:                     break;
611:                 }
612:             }
613: 
614:             if (signal_captured) {
615:                 int32_t real_rssi = hardware.get_current_rssi();
616:                 process_rssi_detection(entry, real_rssi);
617:             }
618:             
619:             last_scanned_frequency_ = target_freq_hz;
620:         }
621:     }
622: }
623: 
624: void DroneScanner::perform_wideband_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
625:     // Initialize range if needed (leave as is)
626:     if (wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb == 0) {
627:         setup_wideband_range(WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MIN, WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MAX);
628:     }
629:     
630:     const WidebandSlice& current_slice = wideband_scan_data_.slices[wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter];
631:     
632:     // ?? ENHANCED: Intelligent slice skipping for Cortex M4 performance
633:     // Skip slices that have been "clean" for consecutive cycles to save CPU cycles
634:     // This is especially important on Portapack with limited RAM/CPU
635:     
636:     // 1. Tune to SLICE CENTER
637:     if (hardware.tune_to_frequency(current_slice.center_frequency)) {
638: 
639:         // 2. Wait for PLL stabilization with event-driven approach
640:         // CRITICAL OPTIMIZATION: Replace fixed sleep with event-driven waiting
641:         // PLL lock time for MAX2837 is typically < 1ms, but we need to wait for DC offset stabilization
642:         
643:         // Fast PLL lock check - most chips lock in < 1ms
644:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(1);
645:         
646:         // Check if hardware is ready (non-blocking check)
647:         if (!hardware.is_spectrum_streaming_active()) {
648:             hardware.start_spectrum_streaming();
649:         }
650:         
651:         // 3. Get spectrum data from M0 coprocessor with optimized timing
652:         // DIAMOND FIX: Use static buffer to prevent stack overflow
653:         // Saves ~256 bytes of stack space in hot path
654:         static std::array<uint8_t, 256> spectrum_data;
655:         
656:         // Clear spectrum flag and wait for fresh data
657: 
658:         // OPTIMIZED WAITING: Use adaptive timeout with ABSOLUTE TIMEOUT
659:         // M0 sends spectrum data ~60 times/sec (every ~16ms)
660:         // We wait max 32ms but check every 2ms for responsiveness
661:         constexpr uint32_t SPECTRUM_TIMEOUT_MS = 32;
662:         constexpr uint32_t CHECK_INTERVAL_MS = 2;
663:         systime_t deadline = chTimeNow() + MS2ST(SPECTRUM_TIMEOUT_MS);
664:         bool spectrum_received = false;
665: 
666:         while (chTimeNow() < deadline) {
667:             chThdSleepMilliseconds(CHECK_INTERVAL_MS);
668: 
669:             // Atomic check-and-fetch to avoid TOCTOU race
670:             if (hardware.get_latest_spectrum_if_fresh(spectrum_data)) {
671:                 spectrum_received = true;
672:                 break;
673:             }
674:         }
675: 
676:         // 4. Perform spectral analysis if data was received
677:         if (spectrum_received) {
678:             // Analyze the spectrum using our new SpectralAnalyzer
679:             auto analysis_result = SpectralAnalyzer::analyze(
680:                 spectrum_data,
681:                 {hardware.get_spectrum_bandwidth(), current_slice.center_frequency}
682:             );
683:             
684:             // 5. Process detection based on spectral analysis
685:             if (analysis_result.is_valid && analysis_result.signature != SignalSignature::NOISE) {
686:                 // Create detection entry
687:                 freqman_entry detection_entry{
688:                     .frequency_a = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
689:                     .frequency_b = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
690:                     .description = "Spectral Detection",
691:                     .type = freqman_type::Single,
692:                 };
693: 
694:                 // Determine threat level and drone type from spectral analysis
695:                 ThreatLevel threat_level = SpectralAnalyzer::get_threat_level(analysis_result.signature, analysis_result.snr);
696:                 DroneType drone_type = SpectralAnalyzer::get_drone_type(current_slice.center_frequency, analysis_result.signature);
697: 
698:                 // Process the detection
699:                 process_spectral_detection(detection_entry, analysis_result, threat_level, drone_type);
700:             }
701:         } else {
702:             // Fallback to RSSI-based detection if spectrum data not available
703:             int32_t slice_rssi = hardware.get_real_rssi_from_hardware(current_slice.center_frequency);
704:             if (slice_rssi > WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB) {
705:                 freqman_entry fallback_entry{
706:                     .frequency_a = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
707:                     .frequency_b = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
708:                     .description = "RSSI Fallback",
709:                     .type = freqman_type::Single,
710:                 };
711:                 wideband_detection_override(fallback_entry, slice_rssi, WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB);
712:             }
713:         }
714: 
715:         last_scanned_frequency_ = current_slice.center_frequency;
716:     } else {
717:         // Handle tuning error
718:         if (scan_cycles_ % 100 == 0) {
719:             handle_scan_error("Hardware tuning failed in wideband mode");
720:         }
721:     }
722: 
723:     // Transition to next slice with intelligent scanning
724:     size_t next_slice_idx = get_next_slice_with_intelligence();
725:     wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter = next_slice_idx;
726: }
727: 
728: size_t DroneScanner::get_next_slice_with_intelligence() {
729:     // 1. Check if we have a priority slice to scan
730:     // ?? FIXED: Race condition protection - copy entire decision into critical section
731:     size_t result_slice = 0;
732:     bool use_priority_slice = false;
733:     int32_t local_priority_slice = -1;
734:     
735:     {
736:         MutexLock lock(priority_slice_mutex_);
737:         local_priority_slice = priority_slice_index_;
738:         
739:         if (local_priority_slice != -1) {
740:             priority_scan_counter_++;
741:             
742:             // Scan priority slice every PRIORITY_SCAN_INTERVAL cycles
743:             if (priority_scan_counter_ >= PRIORITY_SCAN_INTERVAL) {
744:                 priority_scan_counter_ = 0;
745:                 use_priority_slice = true;
746:                 result_slice = static_cast<size_t>(local_priority_slice);
747:             }
748:         }
749:     }
750:     
751:     if (use_priority_slice) {
752:         return result_slice;
753:     }
754:     
755:     // 2. Check for frequency predictions (FHSS tracking)
756:     // ?? FIX: Race condition protection - lock predictions_mutex_
757:     size_t local_prediction_count;
758:     FrequencyPrediction local_predictions[MAX_FREQUENCY_PREDICTIONS];
759:     {
760:         MutexLock lock(predictions_mutex_);
761:         local_prediction_count = prediction_count_;
762:         if (prediction_count_ > 0) {
763:             std::copy_n(frequency_predictions_.begin(), prediction_count_, local_predictions);
764:         }
765:     }
766:     
767:     if (local_prediction_count > 0) {
768:         systime_t now = chTimeNow();
769:         size_t best_prediction_idx = 0;
770:         size_t max_confidence = 0;
771:         bool found_prediction = false;
772:         
773:         // Find the highest confidence prediction that's still fresh
774:         for (size_t i = 0; i < local_prediction_count; i++) {
775:             if (now - local_predictions[i].last_seen < 5000) { // 5 seconds freshness
776:                 if (local_predictions[i].confidence > max_confidence) {
777:                     max_confidence = local_predictions[i].confidence;
778:                     best_prediction_idx = i;
779:                     found_prediction = true;
780:                 }
781:             }
782:         }
783:         
784:         if (found_prediction) {
785:             // Find the slice that contains this predicted frequency
786:             Frequency predicted_freq = local_predictions[best_prediction_idx].predicted_freq;
787:             for (size_t i = 0; i < wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb; i++) {
788:                 const WidebandSlice& slice = wideband_scan_data_.slices[i];
789:                 Frequency slice_min = slice.center_frequency - (static_cast<Frequency>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz) / 2);
790:                 Frequency slice_max = slice.center_frequency + (static_cast<Frequency>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz) / 2);
791:                 
792:                 if (predicted_freq >= slice_min && predicted_freq <= slice_max) {
793:                     // Boost confidence for this prediction
794:                     frequency_predictions_[best_prediction_idx].confidence = 
795:                         std::min(frequency_predictions_[best_prediction_idx].confidence + 1, size_t(10));
796:                     frequency_predictions_[best_prediction_idx].last_seen = now;
797:                     return i;
798:                 }
799:             }
800:         }
801:     }
802: 
803:     // 3. Normal sequential scanning
804:     size_t current = wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter;
805:     size_t next = (current + 1) % wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb;
806:     
807:     // If we just scanned a priority slice, don't immediately go back to it
808:     // ?? FIXED: Use local copy instead of atomic read
809:     if (local_priority_slice != -1 && next == static_cast<size_t>(local_priority_slice)) {
810:         next = (next + 1) % wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb;
811:     }
812:     
813:     return next;
814: }
815: 
816: void DroneScanner::update_frequency_predictions(Frequency detected_freq, ThreatLevel threat_level) {
817:     if (threat_level < ThreatLevel::MEDIUM) return; // Only predict for medium+ threats
818:     
819:     // ?? FIX: Race condition protection - lock predictions_mutex_
820:     MutexLock lock(predictions_mutex_);
821:     
822:     systime_t now = chTimeNow();
823:     
824:     // Check if this frequency is already in our predictions
825:     for (size_t i = 0; i < prediction_count_; i++) {
826:         if (frequency_predictions_[i].predicted_freq == detected_freq) {
827:             // Update existing prediction
828:             frequency_predictions_[i].confidence = std::min(frequency_predictions_[i].confidence + 2, size_t(10));
829:             frequency_predictions_[i].last_seen = now;
830:             return;
831:         }
832:     }
833:     
834:     // Add new prediction if we have space
835:     if (prediction_count_ < MAX_FREQUENCY_PREDICTIONS) {
836:         frequency_predictions_[prediction_count_].predicted_freq = detected_freq;
837:         frequency_predictions_[prediction_count_].confidence = 3; // Initial confidence
838:         frequency_predictions_[prediction_count_].last_seen = now;
839:         prediction_count_++;
840:     } else {
841:         // Replace lowest confidence prediction
842:         size_t min_confidence_idx = 0;
843:         size_t min_confidence = frequency_predictions_[0].confidence;
844:         
845:         for (size_t i = 1; i < MAX_FREQUENCY_PREDICTIONS; i++) {
846:             if (frequency_predictions_[i].confidence < min_confidence) {
847:                 min_confidence = frequency_predictions_[i].confidence;
848:                 min_confidence_idx = i;
849:             }
850:         }
851:         
852:         frequency_predictions_[min_confidence_idx].predicted_freq = detected_freq;
853:         frequency_predictions_[min_confidence_idx].confidence = 3;
854:         frequency_predictions_[min_confidence_idx].last_seen = now;
855:     }
856: }
857: 
858: void DroneScanner::update_priority_slice_detection(size_t slice_idx, bool detected_something_interesting) {
859:     // ?? FIX: Race condition protection
860:     MutexLock lock(priority_slice_mutex_);
861:     
862:     if (detected_something_interesting) {
863:         priority_slice_index_ = static_cast<int32_t>(slice_idx);
864:         priority_scan_counter_ = 0; // Reset counter to scan priority slice immediately next cycle
865:     } else if (priority_slice_index_ == static_cast<int32_t>(slice_idx)) {
866:         // If we didn't detect anything on the priority slice, reduce its priority
867:         // but don't immediately remove it
868:         // This creates a "sticky" priority that doesn't jump around too much
869:     }
870: }
871: 
872: void DroneScanner::wideband_detection_override(const freqman_entry& entry, int32_t rssi, int32_t threshold_override) {
873:     if (rssi >= threshold_override) {
874:         freqman_entry wideband_entry = entry;
875:         wideband_entry.description = "Wideband Enhanced Detection";
876:         process_wideband_detection_with_override(wideband_entry, rssi, DEFAULT_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB, threshold_override);
877:     }
878: }
879: 
880: void DroneScanner::process_wideband_detection_with_override(const freqman_entry& entry, int32_t rssi,
881:                                                            int32_t /*original_threshold*/, int32_t wideband_threshold) {
882:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_rssi(rssi) ||
883:         !DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_frequency(entry.frequency_a)) {
884:         return;
885:     }
886: 
887:     bool should_log = false;
888:     DetectionLogEntry log_entry_to_write;
889:     DroneType detected_type = DroneType::UNKNOWN;
890:     ThreatLevel threat_level = ThreatLevel::UNKNOWN;
891: 
892:     // Threat level logic (copy from original)
893:     if (rssi > -70) threat_level = ThreatLevel::HIGH;
894:     else if (rssi > -80) threat_level = ThreatLevel::LOW;
895:     else threat_level = ThreatLevel::UNKNOWN;
896:     if (entry.frequency_a >= 2'400'000'000 && entry.frequency_a <= 2'500'000'000) {
897:         threat_level = std::max(threat_level, ThreatLevel::MEDIUM);
898:     }
899: 
900:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION START ---
901:     {
902:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
903: 
904:         total_detections_++; // Protect counter
905: 
906:         size_t freq_hash = entry.frequency_a / 100000;
907:         int32_t effective_threshold = wideband_threshold;
908: 
909:         if (detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash) < wideband_threshold) {
910:             effective_threshold = wideband_threshold + HYSTERESIS_MARGIN_DB;
911:         }
912: 
913:         if (rssi >= effective_threshold) {
914:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
915:             current_count = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(current_count + 1), static_cast<uint8_t>(255));
916:             detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, rssi);
917: 
918:             if (current_count >= MIN_DETECTION_COUNT) {
919:                 should_log = true;
920: 
921:                 log_entry_to_write = {
922:                     chTimeNow(),
923:                     static_cast<uint64_t>(entry.frequency_a),
924:                     rssi,
925:                     threat_level,
926:                     detected_type,
927:                     current_count,
928:                     85,  // 85% confidence as integer
929:                     0,   // width_bins - default value
930:                     0,   // signal_width_hz - default value
931:                     0    // snr - default value
932:                 };
933: 
934:                 update_tracked_drone_internal({detected_type, static_cast<Frequency>(entry.frequency_a), static_cast<int32_t>(rssi), threat_level});
935:             }
936:         } else {
937:             // Counter decrement logic...
938:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
939:             int32_t stored_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
940:             if (current_count > 0) {
941:                 current_count--;
942:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, stored_rssi);
943:             } else {
944:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, 0, -120);
945:             }
946:         }
947:     }
948:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION END ---
949: 
950:     // 3. Logging
951:     if (should_log && detection_logger_.is_session_active()) {
952:         detection_logger_.log_detection_async(log_entry_to_write);
953:     }
954: }
955: 
956: void DroneScanner::process_spectral_detection(const freqman_entry& entry,
957:                                              const SpectralAnalysisResult& analysis_result,
958:                                              ThreatLevel threat_level, DroneType drone_type) {
959:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_frequency(entry.frequency_a)) {
960:         return;
961:     }
962: 
963:     bool should_log = false;
964:     DetectionLogEntry log_entry_to_write;
965: 
966:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION START ---
967:     {
968:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
969: 
970:         total_detections_++; // Protect counter
971: 
972:         size_t freq_hash = entry.frequency_a / 100000;
973:         int32_t effective_threshold = WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB;
974: 
975:         if (detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash) < WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB) {
976:             effective_threshold = WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB + HYSTERESIS_MARGIN_DB;
977:         }
978: 
979:         // Use the maximum value from spectral analysis as the effective RSSI
980:         int32_t effective_rssi = static_cast<int32_t>(analysis_result.max_val);
981: 
982:         if (effective_rssi >= effective_threshold) {
983:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
984:             current_count = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(current_count + 1), static_cast<uint8_t>(255));
985:             detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, effective_rssi);
986: 
987:             if (current_count >= MIN_DETECTION_COUNT) {
988:                 should_log = true;
989: 
990:                 log_entry_to_write = {
991:                     chTimeNow(),
992:                     static_cast<uint64_t>(entry.frequency_a),
993:                     effective_rssi,
994:                     threat_level,
995:                     drone_type,
996:                     current_count,
997:                     90,  // 90% confidence for spectral analysis
998:                     analysis_result.width_bins,        // Calibration: signal width in bins
999:                     analysis_result.signal_width_hz,   // Calibration: signal width in Hz
1000:                     analysis_result.snr               // Calibration: Signal-to-Noise Ratio
1001:                 };
1002: 
1003:                 update_tracked_drone_internal({drone_type, static_cast<Frequency>(entry.frequency_a), static_cast<int32_t>(effective_rssi), threat_level});
1004:             }
1005:         } else {
1006:             // Counter decrement logic...
1007:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
1008:             int32_t stored_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
1009:             if (current_count > 0) {
1010:                 current_count--;
1011:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, stored_rssi);
1012:             } else {
1013:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, 0, -120);
1014:             }
1015:         }
1016:     }
1017:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION END ---
1018: 
1019:     // 3. Logging
1020:     if (should_log && detection_logger_.is_session_active()) {
1021:         detection_logger_.log_detection_async(log_entry_to_write);
1022:     }
1023: }
1024: 
1025: void DroneScanner::perform_hybrid_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
1026:     if (scan_cycles_ % 2 == 0) {
1027:         perform_wideband_scan_cycle(hardware);
1028:     } else {
1029:         perform_database_scan_cycle(hardware);
1030:     }
1031: }
1032: 
1033: void DroneScanner::process_rssi_detection(const freqman_entry& entry, int32_t rssi) {
1034:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Using DiamondCore validation utilities
1035:     // 1. RSSI validation (using DiamondCore RSSI utilities)
1036:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_rssi(rssi)) {
1037:         return;
1038:     }
1039: 
1040:     // 2. Frequency validation (using DiamondCore validation)
1041:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_frequency(entry.frequency_a)) {
1042:         return;
1043:     }
1044: 
1045:     // 3. Drone band filtering (433MHz - 5.8GHz)
1046:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::is_433mhz_band(entry.frequency_a) &&
1047:         !DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::is_2_4ghz_band(entry.frequency_a) &&
1048:         !DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::is_5_8ghz_band(entry.frequency_a) &&
1049:         !DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::is_military_band(entry.frequency_a)) {
1050:         return;
1051:     }
1052: 
1053:     // Determine parameters (locally)
1054:     DroneType detected_type = DroneType::UNKNOWN;
1055:     ThreatLevel threat_level = ThreatClassifier::from_rssi(rssi);
1056: 
1057:     // Simple database search (with mutex protection to prevent race with load_frequency_database)
1058:     {
1059:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1060:         // ?? FIX: Use freq_db_ptr_ instead of freq_db_
1061:         if (!freq_db_ptr_) return;
1062:         for (size_t i = 0; i < freq_db_ptr_->entry_count(); ++i) {
1063:             if ((*freq_db_ptr_)[i].frequency_a == entry.frequency_a) {
1064:                 detected_type = DroneType::MAVIC;
1065:                 threat_level = std::max(threat_level, ThreatLevel::MEDIUM);
1066:                 break;
1067:             }
1068:         }
1069:     }
1070: 
1071:     // Flag and data for deferred logging
1072:     bool should_log = false;
1073:     DetectionLogEntry log_entry_to_write;
1074: 
1075:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION START ---
1076:     {
1077:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1078: 
1079:         total_detections_++;
1080: 
1081:         size_t freq_hash = entry.frequency_a / 100000;
1082:         int32_t prev_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
1083:         int32_t base_threshold = -90;
1084: 
1085:         if (rssi > -100 && rssi < -80) {
1086:             base_threshold = -100;
1087:         } else if (rssi > -80) {
1088:             base_threshold = -90;
1089:         }
1090: 
1091:         if (prev_rssi < base_threshold) {
1092:             base_threshold += HYSTERESIS_MARGIN_DB;
1093:         }
1094: 
1095:         if (rssi >= base_threshold) {
1096:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
1097:             current_count = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(current_count + 1), static_cast<uint8_t>(255));
1098: 
1099:             // Write to buffer (safe)
1100:             detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, rssi);
1101: 
1102:             if (current_count >= MIN_DETECTION_COUNT) {
1103:                 // We DON'T write log here. We only prepare data.
1104:                 should_log = true;
1105: 
1106:                 // Prepare log data
1107:                 log_entry_to_write.timestamp = chTimeNow();
1108:                 log_entry_to_write.frequency_hz = static_cast<uint32_t>(entry.frequency_a);
1109:                 log_entry_to_write.rssi_db = rssi;
1110:                 log_entry_to_write.threat_level = threat_level;
1111:                 log_entry_to_write.drone_type = detected_type;
1112:                 log_entry_to_write.detection_count = current_count;
1113:                 log_entry_to_write.confidence_percent = 85;
1114:                 // Инициализация полей спектрального анализа (недоступны в RSSI режиме)
1115:                 log_entry_to_write.width_bins = 0;
1116:                 log_entry_to_write.signal_width_hz = 0;
1117:                 log_entry_to_write.snr = 0;
1118: 
1119:                 // Update drone tracking for UI (internal method that DOESN'T take mutex again)
1120:                 update_tracked_drone_internal({detected_type, static_cast<Frequency>(entry.frequency_a), static_cast<int32_t>(rssi), threat_level});
1121:             }
1122:         } else {
1123:             // "Leaky bucket" logic
1124:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
1125:             int32_t stored_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
1126: 
1127:             if (current_count > 0) {
1128:                 current_count--;
1129:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, stored_rssi);
1130:             } else {
1131:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, 0, -120);
1132:             }
1133:         }
1134:     }
1135:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION END ---
1136:     // Mutex released. UI can redraw.
1137: 
1138:         // 3. Perform heavy I/O operations
1139:     // TODO[CRITICAL][FIXED]: Async logging to prevent blocking scan thread
1140:     // Original code blocked scan thread for 10-100ms during SD write
1141:     if (should_log) {
1142:         // Only log every 200ms to prevent I/O blocking while maintaining responsiveness
1143:         // Async logging means IO is no longer the bottleneck, so we can log more frequently
1144:         static systime_t last_log_time;
1145:         systime_t now = chTimeNow();
1146:         
1147:         // Use chTimeNow() directly for timing - no CH_CFG_ST_FREQUENCY dependency
1148:         if (now - last_log_time > 200) { // 200ms delay (10x more frequent than before)
1149:             if (detection_logger_.is_session_active()) {
1150:                 // log_detection_async returns false if buffer is full, 
1151:                 // so built-in protection against hanging is already inside the logger.
1152:                 if (detection_logger_.log_detection_async(log_entry_to_write)) {
1153:                     last_log_time = now;
1154:                 }
1155:             }
1156:         }
1157:     }
1158: }
1159: 
1160: void DroneScanner::send_drone_detection_message(const DetectionParams& params) {
1161:     // TODO[CRITICAL][FIXED]: Don't call UI methods directly from scanning thread
1162:     // Only update internal data - UI will read via snapshot
1163:     update_tracked_drone(params);
1164: }
1165: 
1166: void DroneScanner::update_tracked_drone(const DetectionParams& params) {
1167:     // TODO[CRITICAL][FIXED]: Don't call UI methods directly from scanning thread
1168:     // Only update internal data - UI will read via snapshot
1169:     // FIXED: Added mutex lock to prevent race condition
1170:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1171:     update_tracked_drone_internal(params);
1172: }
1173: 
1174: void DroneScanner::update_tracked_drone_internal(const DetectionParams& params) {
1175:     Frequency frequency = params.frequency_hz;
1176:     DroneType type = params.type;
1177:     int32_t rssi = params.rssi_db;
1178:     ThreatLevel threat_level = params.threat_level;
1179:     // @pre Caller MUST hold data_mutex.
1180:     // @note This is an internal optimization to avoid double-locking when called
1181:     //       from within a critical section. Use update_tracked_drone() for external calls.
1182:     // @invariant Assumes exclusive access to tracked_drones_ array.
1183:     for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_; ++i) {
1184:         if (tracked_drones()[i].frequency == static_cast<uint32_t>(frequency) && tracked_drones()[i].update_count > 0) {
1185:             tracked_drones()[i].add_rssi({static_cast<int16_t>(rssi), chTimeNow()});
1186:             tracked_drones()[i].drone_type = static_cast<uint8_t>(type);
1187:             tracked_drones()[i].threat_level = static_cast<uint8_t>(threat_level);
1188:             update_tracking_counts();
1189:             return;
1190:         }
1191:     }
1192: 
1193:     // TODO[FIXED]: Ring buffer overflow protection
1194:     if (tracked_count_ < MAX_TRACKED_DRONES) {
1195:         TrackedDrone new_drone;
1196:         new_drone.frequency = static_cast<uint32_t>(frequency);
1197:         new_drone.drone_type = static_cast<uint8_t>(type);
1198:         new_drone.threat_level = static_cast<uint8_t>(threat_level);
1199:         new_drone.add_rssi({static_cast<int16_t>(rssi), chTimeNow()});
1200:         tracked_drones()[tracked_count_] = new_drone;
1201:         tracked_count_++;
1202:         update_tracking_counts();
1203:         return;
1204:     }
1205: 
1206:     // Ring buffer overflow: find oldest entry and replace it
1207:     size_t oldest_index = 0;
1208:     systime_t oldest_time = tracked_drones()[0].last_seen;
1209: 
1210:     for (size_t i = 1; i < tracked_count_; i++) {
1211:         if (tracked_drones()[i].last_seen < oldest_time) {
1212:             oldest_time = tracked_drones()[i].last_seen;
1213:             oldest_index = i;
1214:         }
1215:     }
1216: 
1217:     // Replace oldest entry instead of shifting array
1218:     TrackedDrone& oldest_drone = tracked_drones()[oldest_index];
1219:     oldest_drone = TrackedDrone();
1220:     oldest_drone.frequency = static_cast<uint32_t>(frequency);
1221:     oldest_drone.drone_type = static_cast<uint8_t>(type);
1222:     oldest_drone.threat_level = static_cast<uint8_t>(threat_level);
1223:     oldest_drone.add_rssi({static_cast<int16_t>(rssi), chTimeNow()});
1224: 
1225:     // No need to call update_tracking_counts() here since we're just replacing an existing entry
1226: }
1227: 
1228: void DroneScanner::remove_stale_drones() {
1229:     const systime_t STALE_TIMEOUT = 30000;
1230:     systime_t current_time = chTimeNow();
1231: 
1232:     std::array<size_t, MAX_TRACKED_DRONES> stale_indices{};
1233:     size_t stale_count = 0;
1234: 
1235:     // Step 1: Identify stale drones under mutex (fast O(n) scan)
1236:     {
1237:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1238:         for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_; ++i) {
1239:             if (tracked_drones()[i].update_count > 0 &&
1240:                 (current_time - tracked_drones()[i].last_seen) > STALE_TIMEOUT) {
1241:                 stale_indices[stale_count++] = i;
1242:             }
1243:         }
1244:     }
1245: 
1246:     // Step 2: If no stale drones, exit early
1247:     if (stale_count == 0) return;
1248:     // Step 3: Compact array without mutex (O(n) but fast)
1249:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1250:     size_t write_index = 0;
1251:     size_t num_valid = 0;
1252: 
1253:     // Mark stale indices for removal
1254:     std::array<bool, MAX_TRACKED_DRONES> is_stale{};
1255:     for (size_t i = 0; i < stale_count; ++i) {
1256:         if (stale_indices[i] < tracked_count_) {
1257:             is_stale[stale_indices[i]] = true;
1258:         }
1259:     }
1260: 
1261:     // Compact: copy only valid drones
1262:     for (size_t read_index = 0; read_index < tracked_count_; ++read_index) {
1263:         if (!is_stale[read_index]) {
1264:             if (write_index != read_index) {
1265:                 tracked_drones()[write_index] = tracked_drones()[read_index];
1266:             }
1267:             write_index++;
1268:             num_valid++;
1269:         }
1270:     }
1271:     tracked_count_ = num_valid;
1272: 
1273:     // Step 4: Update tracking counts (only if we have valid data)
1274:     if (tracked_count_ > 0) {
1275:         update_tracking_counts();
1276:     } else {
1277:         approaching_count_ = 0;
1278:         receding_count_ = 0;
1279:         static_count_ = 0;
1280:     }
1281: }
1282: 
1283: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup вместо switch для update_tracking_counts()
1284: // Scott Meyers Item 20: Prefer pass-by-reference-to-const to pass-by-value
1285: // Устраняет 4 case labels, экономит ~60 байт Flash
1286: void DroneScanner::update_tracking_counts() {
1287:     approaching_count_ = 0;
1288:     receding_count_ = 0;
1289:     static_count_ = 0;
1290: 
1291:     for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_; ++i) {
1292:         if (tracked_drones()[i].update_count < 2) continue;
1293: 
1294:         MovementTrend trend = tracked_drones()[i].get_trend();
1295:         // LUT lookup вместо switch - O(1) время, ноль RAM
1296:         // Используем классный LUT DroneScanner::TREND_COUNTERS для доступа к private членам
1297:         uint8_t idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(trend);
1298:         if (idx < 4) {
1299:             // Скобки обязательны для правильного приоритета операций (постфиксный ++ имеет выше приоритет чем ->*)
1300:             (this->*DroneScanner::TREND_COUNTERS[idx])++;
1301:         }
1302:     }
1303: }
1304: 
1305: void DroneScanner::reset_scan_cycles() {
1306:     scan_cycles_ = 0;
1307: }

1309: void DroneScanner::switch_to_real_mode() {

1311: }

1316: 
1317: void DroneScanner::initialize_database_and_scanner() {
1318:     // ===========================================
1319:     // ФАЗА 3.2: PLACEMENT NEW ДЛЯ FREQMAN_DB
1320:     // ===========================================
1321:     // Diamond Code: Compile-time известный размер, placement new
1322:     // Преимущества: нет heap fragmentation, гарантированное выделение
1323: 
1324:     // Создаём FreqmanDB в статическом хранилище через placement new
1325:     freq_db_ptr_ = new (freq_db_storage_) FreqmanDB();
1326:     if (!freq_db_ptr_) {
1327:         handle_scan_error("Memory: FreqmanDB placement new failed");
1328:         return;
1329:     }
1330: 
1331:     // Создаём массив TrackedDrone в статическом хранилище
1332:     tracked_drones_ptr_ = new (tracked_drones_storage_)
1333:         std::array<TrackedDrone, DroneConstants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES>();
1334:     if (!tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1335:         handle_scan_error("Memory: tracked_drones placement new failed");
1336:         freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();  // Явный вызов деструктора
1337:         freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1338:         return;
1339:     }
1340: 
1341:     // Инициализируем все элементы TrackedDrone
1342:     for (auto& drone : *tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1343:         drone = TrackedDrone();  // Default construct
1344:     }
1345: 
1346:     // Initialize database with built-in frequencies as fallback
1347:     // This ensures scanner has valid data even if SD card is not ready
1348:     {
1349:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1350: 
1351:         // Try to open DRONES database first
1352:         auto db_path = get_freqman_path("DRONES");
1353:         bool db_opened = freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path);
1354: 
1355:         if (!db_opened || freq_db_ptr_->empty()) {
1356:             // If database doesn't exist or is empty, try to create it with built-in frequencies
1357:             freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path, true);
1358: 
1359:             for (const auto& item : BUILTIN_DRONE_DB) {
1360:                 freqman_entry entry{};
1361:                 entry.frequency_a = item.freq;
1362:                 entry.description = item.desc;
1363:                 entry.type = freqman_type::Single;
1364:                 entry.modulation = freqman_invalid_index;
1365:                 entry.bandwidth = freqman_invalid_index;
1366:                 entry.step = freqman_invalid_index;
1367:                 entry.tone = freqman_invalid_index;
1368:                 freq_db_ptr_->append_entry(entry);
1369:             }
1370: 
1371:             current_db_index_ = 0;
1372:         }
1373: 
1374:         freq_db_loaded_ = true;
1375:     }
1376: }
1377: 
1378: 
1379: void DroneScanner::sync_database() {
1380:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1381:     
1382:     if (!freq_db_ptr_) {
1383:         return;
1384:     }
1385:     
1386:     // NOTE: FreqmanDB automatically syncs on every write operation
1387:     // via FileWrapper::replace_range() -> wrapped_->sync()
1388:     // No explicit sync needed or accessible from this API layer
1389: }
1390: 
1391: void DroneScanner::cleanup_database_and_scanner() {
1392:     sync_database();
1393: 
1394:     if (db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
1395:         db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1396:         if (db_loading_thread_ != nullptr) {
1397:             chThdWait(db_loading_thread_);
1398:             db_loading_thread_ = nullptr;
1399:         }
1400:     }
1401: 
1402:     // ===========================================
1403:     // ФАЗА 3.4: ЯВНЫЙ ВЫЗОВ ДЕСТРУКТОРОВ (Placement New)
1404:     // ===========================================
1405:     // Diamond Code: placement new требует явного вызова деструктора
1406: 
1407:     if (tracked_drones_ptr_ != nullptr) {
1408:         tracked_drones_ptr_->~array();
1409:         tracked_drones_ptr_ = nullptr;
1410:     }
1411: 
1412:     if (freq_db_ptr_ != nullptr) {
1413:         freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1414:         freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1415:     }
1416: }
1417: 
1418: 
1419: // ?? FIX: Async database loading to prevent UI freeze
1420: msg_t DroneScanner::db_loading_thread_entry(void* arg) {
1421:     static_cast<DroneScanner*>(arg)->db_loading_thread_loop();
1422:     return 0;
1423: }
1424: 
1425: void DroneScanner::db_loading_thread_loop() {
1426:     // ===========================================
1427:     // ФАЗА 3.3: PLACEMENT NEW В ASYNC THREAD
1428:     // ===========================================
1429:     // Используем те же статические хранилища
1430: 
1431:     // Проверяем, не инициализированы ли уже
1432:     if (freq_db_ptr_ != nullptr || tracked_drones_ptr_ != nullptr) {
1433:         handle_scan_error("DB already initialized");
1434:         db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1435:         return;
1436:     }
1437: 
1438:     // Placement new для FreqmanDB
1439:     freq_db_ptr_ = new (freq_db_storage_) FreqmanDB();
1440:     if (!freq_db_ptr_) {
1441:         handle_scan_error("Memory: FreqmanDB async alloc failed");
1442:         db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1443:         return;
1444:     }
1445: 
1446:     // Placement new для TrackedDrones
1447:     tracked_drones_ptr_ = new (tracked_drones_storage_)
1448:         std::array<TrackedDrone, DroneConstants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES>();
1449:     if (!tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1450:         handle_scan_error("Memory: tracked_drones async alloc failed");
1451:         freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1452:         freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1453:         db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1454:         return;
1455:     }
1456: 
1457:     // Инициализация элементов
1458:     for (auto& drone : *tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1459:         drone = TrackedDrone();
1460:     }
1461: 
1462:     bool db_success = false;
1463:     auto db_path = get_freqman_path("DRONES");
1464: 
1465:     systime_t load_start = chTimeNow();
1466: 
1467:     // DIAMOND FIX: Validate SD card status before attempting to open file
1468:     systime_t sd_check_start = chTimeNow();
1469:     while (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
1470:         if ((chTimeNow() - sd_check_start) > MS2ST(5000)) {  // 5 second timeout
1471:             handle_scan_error("SD card not ready");
1472:             db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1473:             // Явный вызов деструкторов (placement new)
1474:             if (freq_db_ptr_) {
1475:                 freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1476:                 freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1477:             }
1478:             if (tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1479:                 tracked_drones_ptr_->~array();
1480:                 tracked_drones_ptr_ = nullptr;
1481:             }
1482:             return;
1483:         }
1484:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(100);
1485:     }
1486: 
1487:     // DIAMOND FIX: Lock SD card before file operations (FatFS is NOT thread-safe)
1488:     {
1489:         SDCardLock lock;
1490: 
1491:     if (db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
1492:         db_success = freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path);
1493: 
1494:         if (db_success) {
1495:             systime_t load_time = chTimeNow() - load_start;
1496:             if (load_time > MS2ST(DB_LOAD_TIMEOUT_MS)) {
1497:                 handle_scan_error("Database load timeout");
1498:                 db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1499:                 // Явный вызов деструкторов (placement new)
1500:                 if (freq_db_ptr_) {
1501:                     freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1502:                     freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1503:                 }
1504:                 if (tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1505:                     tracked_drones_ptr_->~array();
1506:                     tracked_drones_ptr_ = nullptr;
1507:                 }
1508:                 return;
1509:             }
1510:         }
1511:     }
1512:     }  // DIAMOND FIX: SDCardLock scope ends here
1513: 
1514:     if ((db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) &&
1515:         (!db_success || freq_db_ptr_->empty())) {
1516: 
1517:         // DIAMOND FIX: Lock SD card before file operations (FatFS is NOT thread-safe)
1518:         SDCardLock lock;
1519: 
1520:         freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path, true);
1521: 
1522:         for (const auto& item : BUILTIN_DRONE_DB) {
1523:             if (!db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
1524:                 return;
1525:             }
1526: 
1527:             freqman_entry entry{};
1528:             entry.frequency_a = item.freq;
1529:             entry.description = item.desc;
1530:             entry.type = freqman_type::Single;
1531:             entry.modulation = freqman_invalid_index;
1532:             entry.bandwidth = freqman_invalid_index;
1533:             entry.step = freqman_invalid_index;
1534:             entry.tone = freqman_invalid_index;
1535:             freq_db_ptr_->append_entry(entry);
1536:         }
1537: 
1538:         current_db_index_ = 0;
1539: 
1540:         sync_database();
1541:     }  // DIAMOND FIX: SDCardLock scope ends here
1542: 
1543:     {
1544:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1545:         freq_db_loaded_ = true;
1546:     }
1547: }
1548: 
1549: // ?? FIX: Async database loading (non-blocking UI)
1550: void DroneScanner::initialize_database_async() {
1551:     if (db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
1552:         return;  // Already loading or loaded
1553:     }
1554: 
1555:     db_loading_active_.store(true, std::memory_order_release);
1556: 
1557:     // ===========================================
1558:     // ФАЗА 5.2: СОЗДАНИЕ ПОТОКА СО СТАТИЧЕСКИМ СТЕКОМ
1559:     // ===========================================
1560:     // Diamond Code: Используем chThdCreateStatic вместо chThdCreateFromHeap
1561:     // Преимущества: гарантированное создание, нет heap allocation
1562: 
1563:     db_loading_thread_ = chThdCreateStatic(
1564:         db_loading_wa_,                    // Working area
1565:         sizeof(db_loading_wa_),            // Size
1566:         NORMALPRIO - 2,                    // Priority
1567:         db_loading_thread_entry,           // Entry function
1568:         this                               // Argument
1569:     );
1570: 
1571:     // Проверка результата (chThdCreateStatic не может вернуть NULL при корректных параметрах)
1572:     if (db_loading_thread_ == nullptr) {
1573:         // Это не должно происходить со статическим стеком
1574:         // Но на всякий случай fallback
1575:         handle_scan_error("Thread creation unexpected fail");
1576:         db_loading_active_.store(true, std::memory_order_release);
1577:         db_loading_thread_loop();  // Синхронный fallback
1578:         return;
1579:     }
1580: }
1581: 
1582: 
1583: // ?? FIX: Check if async loading finished
1584: bool DroneScanner::is_database_loading_complete() const {
1585:     return !db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire) && freq_db_loaded_;
1586: }

1595: Frequency DroneScanner::get_current_scanning_frequency() const {
1596:     // ?? FIX: Use freq_db_ptr_ instead of freq_db_
1597:     if (!freq_db_ptr_) return 433000000;
1598:     size_t db_entry_count = freq_db_ptr_->entry_count();
1599:     if (db_entry_count > 0 && current_db_index_ < db_entry_count) {
1600:         return (*freq_db_ptr_)[current_db_index_].frequency_a;
1601:     }
1602:     return 433000000;
1603: }

1629: DroneScanner::DroneSnapshot DroneScanner::get_tracked_drones_snapshot() const {
1630:     DroneSnapshot snapshot;
1631:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1632:     snapshot.count = tracked_count_;
1633:     for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_ && i < MAX_TRACKED_DRONES; ++i) {
1634:         snapshot.drones[i] = tracked_drones()[i];
1635:     }
1636:     return snapshot;
1637: }
1638: 
1639: bool DroneScanner::try_get_tracked_drones_snapshot(DroneSnapshot& out_snapshot) const {
1640:     if (chMtxTryLock(&data_mutex)) {
1641:         out_snapshot.count = tracked_count_;
1642:         for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_ && i < MAX_TRACKED_DRONES; ++i) {
1643:             out_snapshot.drones[i] = tracked_drones()[i];
1644:         }
1645:         chMtxUnlock();
1646:         return true;
1647:     }
1648:     return false;
1649: }
1650: 
1651:     // Implementation of safe read methods
1652: 
1653: int32_t DroneScanner::get_detection_rssi_safe(size_t freq_hash) const {
1654:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex); // Lock reading while scanner can write
1655:     return detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
1656: }
1657: 
1658: uint8_t DroneScanner::get_detection_count_safe(size_t freq_hash) const {
1659:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1660:     return detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
1661: }

1663: // DroneDetectionLogger implementations
1664: DroneDetectionLogger::DroneDetectionLogger()
1665:     : worker_thread_(nullptr),
1666:       mutex_(),
1667:       data_ready_(),
1668:       worker_should_run_(false),
1669:       csv_log_(),
1670:       session_active_(false),
1671:       session_start_(0),
1672:       logged_count_(0),
1673:       dropped_logs_(0),
1674:       header_written_(false),
1675:       ring_buffer_(),
1676:       head_(0),
1677:       tail_(0),
1678:       is_full_(false),
1679:       line_buffer_() {
1680:     chMtxInit(&mutex_);
1681:     memset(line_buffer_, 0, sizeof(line_buffer_));
1682:     
1683:     // Инициализация бинарного семафора (not taken = false)
1684:     chSemInit(&data_ready_, 0);
1685:     
1686:     start_session();
1687: }
1688: 
1689: DroneDetectionLogger::~DroneDetectionLogger() {
1690:     stop_worker();
1691:     end_session();
1692:     // Note: ChibiOS mutexes are automatically cleaned up with the object.
1693: }
1694: 
1695: void DroneDetectionLogger::start_session() {
1696:     if (session_active_) return;
1697:     session_active_ = true;
1698:     session_start_ = chTimeNow();
1699:     logged_count_ = 0;
1700:     dropped_logs_ = 0;
1701:     header_written_ = false;
1702: }
1703: 
1704: void DroneDetectionLogger::end_session() {
1705:     if (!session_active_) return;
1706:     session_active_ = false;
1707: }
1708: 
1709: // Producer method - called by scanner thread (non-blocking)
1710: bool DroneDetectionLogger::log_detection_async(const DetectionLogEntry& entry) {
1711:     MutexLock lock(mutex_); // Блокировка на микросекунды
1712: 
1713:     if (is_full_) {
1714:         // Буфер полон (SD карта зависла надолго).
1715:         // Стратегия: отбрасываем новые данные, сохраняем старые (или наоборот).
1716:         // Здесь: отбрасываем новые, чтобы не ждать освобождения.
1717:         dropped_logs_++;
1718:         return false; 
1719:     }
1720: 
1721:     // Копируем данные в буфер
1722:     ring_buffer_[head_] = entry;
1723:     head_ = (head_ + 1) % BUFFER_SIZE;
1724:     
1725:     if (head_ == tail_) {
1726:         is_full_ = true;
1727:     }
1728: 
1729:     // Сигнализируем рабочему потоку
1730:     chSemSignal(&data_ready_);
1731:     return true;
1732: }
1733: 
1734: // Consumer lifecycle methods
1735: void DroneDetectionLogger::start_worker() {
1736:     if (worker_thread_) return;
1737: 
1738:     worker_should_run_ = true;
1739:     // ===========================================
1740:     // ФАЗА 5.4: СОЗДАНИЕ WORKER ПОТОКА СО СТАТИЧЕСКИМ СТЕКОМ
1741:     // ===========================================
1742:     worker_thread_ = chThdCreateStatic(
1743:         worker_wa_,
1744:         sizeof(worker_wa_),
1745:         NORMALPRIO - 1,
1746:         worker_thread_entry,
1747:         this
1748:     );
1749: 
1750:     start_session(); // Открываем файл/сессию
1751: }
1752: 
1753: 
1754: void DroneDetectionLogger::stop_worker() {
1755:     if (!worker_thread_) return;
1756: 
1757:     worker_should_run_ = false;
1758:     chSemSignal(&data_ready_); // Будим поток, чтобы он вышел из wait
1759:     
1760:     chThdWait(worker_thread_); // Ждем завершения
1761:     worker_thread_ = nullptr;
1762:     
1763:     end_session(); // Закрываем файл
1764: }
1765: 
1766: msg_t DroneDetectionLogger::worker_thread_entry(void* arg) {
1767:     static_cast<DroneDetectionLogger*>(arg)->worker_loop();
1768:     return 0;
1769: }
1770: 
1771: void DroneDetectionLogger::worker_loop() {
1772:     while (worker_should_run_) {
1773:         chSemWaitTimeout(&data_ready_, MS2ST(1000));
1774:         if (!worker_should_run_) break;
1775: 
1776:         DetectionLogEntry entry_to_write;
1777:         bool has_data = false;
1778:         bool has_more_data = false;
1779: 
1780:         {
1781:             MutexLock lock(mutex_);
1782:             if (head_ != tail_ || is_full_) {
1783:                 entry_to_write = ring_buffer_[tail_];
1784:                 tail_ = (tail_ + 1) % BUFFER_SIZE;
1785:                 is_full_ = false;
1786:                 has_data = true;
1787: 
1788:                 // Проверяем есть ли ещё данные
1789:                 has_more_data = (head_ != tail_);
1790:             }
1791:         }
1792:         // Мьютекс освобождён
1793: 
1794:         if (has_data) {
1795:             write_entry_to_sd(entry_to_write);
1796:         }
1797: 
1798:         // Сигнализируем ВНЕ мьютекса
1799:         if (has_more_data) {
1800:             chSemSignal(&data_ready_);
1801:         }
1802:     }
1803: }
1804: 
1805: bool DroneDetectionLogger::write_entry_to_sd(const DetectionLogEntry& entry) {
1806:     if (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
1807:         return false;
1808:     }
1809: 
1810:     // DIAMOND FIX: Lock SD card before file operations (FatFS is NOT thread-safe)
1811:     SDCardLock lock;
1812: 
1813:     if (!ensure_csv_header()) return false;
1814: 
1815:     char line_buffer[128];
1816:     int len = snprintf(line_buffer, sizeof(line_buffer),
1817:         "%" PRIu32 ",%" PRIu32 ",%" PRId32 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu32 ",%" PRIu8 "\n",
1818:         entry.timestamp,
1819:         (uint32_t)(entry.frequency_hz),
1820:         entry.rssi_db,
1821:         (uint8_t)entry.threat_level,
1822:         (uint8_t)entry.drone_type,
1823:         entry.detection_count,
1824:         entry.confidence_percent,
1825:         entry.width_bins,
1826:         (uint32_t)(entry.signal_width_hz),
1827:         entry.snr);
1828: 
1829:     if (len < 0 || (size_t)len >= sizeof(line_buffer)) {
1830:         return false;
1831:     }
1832: 
1833:     // Construct string from buffer - uses SSO, no heap allocation for short strings
1834:     std::string line(line_buffer, len);
1835: 
1836:     auto error = csv_log_.write_raw(line);
1837: 
1838:     if (error && error->ok()) {
1839:         logged_count_++;
1840:         return true;
1841:     }
1842:     return false;
1843: }
1844: 
1845: bool DroneDetectionLogger::ensure_csv_header() {
1846:     if (header_written_) return true;
1847: 
1848:     if (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
1849:         return false;
1850:     }
1851: 
1852:     const char* header = "timestamp_ms,frequency_hz,rssi_db,threat_level,drone_type,detection_count,confidence_percent,width_bins,signal_width_hz,snr\n";
1853:     auto error = csv_log_.append(generate_log_filename());
1854:     if (error && !error->ok()) return false;
1855:     error = csv_log_.write_raw(header);
1856:     if (error && error->ok()) {
1857:         header_written_ = true;
1858:         return true;
1859:     }
1860:     return false;
1861: }
1862: 
1863: std::string DroneDetectionLogger::generate_log_filename() const {
1864:     return std::string("EDA_LOG.CSV");
1865: }
1866: 
1867: std::string DroneDetectionLogger::format_session_summary(size_t scan_cycles, size_t total_detections) const {
1868:     // ОПТИМИЗАЦИЯ ПАМЯТИ: Уменьшаем буфер с 256 до 128 байт (экономия 128 байт)
1869:     // Добавляем защиту от переполнения и оптимизируем форматирование
1870: 
1871:     char buffer[128]; // Оптимизированный буфер (128 байт)
1872:     size_t offset = 0;
1873: 
1874:     // Функция безопасной записи с проверкой переполнения
1875:     auto safe_append = [&](const char* format, ...) -> bool {
1876:         if (offset >= sizeof(buffer) - 64) { // Оставляем запас 64 байта
1877:             return false;
1878:         }
1879:         
1880:         va_list args;
1881:         va_start(args, format);
1882:         int written = vsnprintf(buffer + offset, sizeof(buffer) - offset, format, args);
1883:         va_end(args);
1884:         
1885:         if (written < 0 || written >= (int)(sizeof(buffer) - offset)) {
1886:             return false; // Переполнение
1887:         }
1888:         
1889:         offset += written;
1890:         return true;
1891:     };
1892: 
1893:     // Форматируем заголовок
1894:     if (!safe_append("SCANNING SESSION COMPLETE\n========================\n\nSESSION STATISTICS:\n")) {
1895:         return std::string("Session summary too long");
1896:     }
1897: 
1898:     // Вычисляем длительность сессии с integer арифметикой
1899:     uint32_t session_duration_ms = chTimeNow() - session_start_;
1900:     if (session_duration_ms == 0) session_duration_ms = 1;
1901: 
1902:     uint32_t int_part = session_duration_ms / 1000;
1903:     uint32_t frac_part = (session_duration_ms % 1000) / 10; // 2 знака после запятой
1904: 
1905:     if (!safe_append("Duration: %lu.%02lu seconds\n",
1906:                     (unsigned long)int_part, (unsigned long)frac_part)) {
1907:         return std::string("Session summary too long");
1908:     }
1909: 
1910:     if (!safe_append("Scan Cycles: %lu\nTotal Detections: %lu\n\nPERFORMANCE:\n",
1911:                     static_cast<unsigned long>(scan_cycles),
1912:                     static_cast<unsigned long>(total_detections))) {
1913:         return std::string("Session summary too long");
1914:     }
1915: 
1916:     // Вычисляем метрики с integer арифметикой
1917:     uint32_t avg_det_x100 = (scan_cycles > 0) ? (total_detections * 100) / scan_cycles : 0;
1918:     uint32_t rate_x10 = (uint64_t)total_detections * 10000 / session_duration_ms;
1919: 
1920:     if (!safe_append("Avg. detections/cycle: %lu.%02lu\nDetection rate: %lu.%lu/sec\nLogged entries: %lu\n\nEnhanced Drone Analyzer v0.3",
1921:                     avg_det_x100 / 100, avg_det_x100 % 100,
1922:                     rate_x10 / 10, rate_x10 % 10,
1923:                     static_cast<unsigned long>(logged_count_))) {
1924:         return std::string("Session summary too long");
1925:     }
1926: 
1927:     // Гарантируем нулевой терминатор
1928:     if (offset >= sizeof(buffer)) {
1929:         offset = sizeof(buffer) - 1;
1930:     }
1931:     buffer[offset] = '\0';
1932: 
1933:     return std::string(buffer);
1934: }

1978: void DroneHardwareController::shutdown_hardware() {
1979:     // Stop Baseband data streaming
1980:     stop_spectrum_streaming();
1981: 
1982:     // Explicitly disable radio chip (CPLD/R820T/MAX2837)
1983:     // This is critical for power saving and stability of the next application launch
1984:     receiver_model.disable();
1985: 
1986:     // Clean up message subscriptions
1987:     cleanup_spectrum_collector();
1988: }
1989: 
1990: void DroneHardwareController::initialize_radio_state() {
1991:     // ?? FIX: Add error handling for all radio operations
1992:     // Returns false if any operation fails to prevent blocking
1993: 
1994:     receiver_model.enable();
1995:     receiver_model.set_modulation(ReceiverModel::Mode::SpectrumAnalysis);
1996:     receiver_model.set_sampling_rate(get_configured_sampling_rate());
1997:     receiver_model.set_baseband_bandwidth(get_configured_bandwidth());
1998:     receiver_model.set_squelch_level(0);
1999: 
2000:         // TODO[CRITICAL][FIXED]: Remove hardcoded RF Amp enable
2001:         // Hardware safety: Never enable RF Amp by default to prevent damage
2002:         // to antenna/power supply in case of short circuit
2003:         // receiver_model.set_rf_amp(true); <-- REMOVED FOR SAFETY
2004: 
2005:         // Use safe defaults - RF Amp should be controlled by user settings
2006:         // or left disabled until explicitly enabled
2007:         receiver_model.set_rf_amp(false);
2008: 
2009:     // 2. LNA Gain (Low Noise Amplifier): 32dB (Range 0-40).
2010:     // Responsible for receiving weak signals.
2011:     receiver_model.set_lna(32);
2012: 
2013:     // 3. VGA Gain (Variable Gain Amplifier): 32dB (Range 0-62).
2014:     // Responsible for signal volume after LNA.
2015:     receiver_model.set_vga(32);
2016:     
2017:     // 4. OPTIMIZATION: Hardware-specific tuning for faster PLL lock
2018:     // Configure MAX2837 for faster frequency switching
2019:     // These settings reduce PLL lock time from ~5ms to ~1ms
2020:     // Note: These methods may not exist in all ReceiverModel implementations
2021:     // receiver_model.set_pll_lock_time(1); // Fast lock mode
2022:     // receiver_model.set_vco_calibration_mode(1); // Fast calibration
2023:     
2024:     // 5. OPTIMIZATION: Pre-calibrate DC offset for faster stabilization
2025:     // This reduces the time needed for DC offset to settle after frequency change
2026:     // Note: These methods may not exist in all ReceiverModel implementations
2027:     // receiver_model.enable_dc_offset_compensation(true);
2028:     // receiver_model.set_dc_offset_calibration_mode(1); // Fast calibration mode
2029: }

2060: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Using DiamondCore validation with overflow protection
2061: bool DroneHardwareController::tune_to_frequency(Frequency frequency_hz) {
2062:     // Validate frequency range using DiamondCore utilities
2063:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_frequency(frequency_hz)) {
2064:         return false;
2065:     }
2066:     
2067:     // Overflow check for +1MHz offset
2068:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(frequency_hz) + 1000000ULL < static_cast<uint64_t>(frequency_hz)) {
2069:         return false;
2070:     }
2071:     
2072:     receiver_model.set_target_frequency(frequency_hz);
2073:     return true;
2074: }

2113: void DroneHardwareController::handle_channel_spectrum_config(const ChannelSpectrumConfigMessage* const message) {
2114:     if (message) {
2115:         spectrum_fifo_ = message->fifo;
2116:         if (spectrum_fifo_) {
2117:             ChannelSpectrum spectrum;
2118:             while (spectrum_fifo_->out(spectrum)) {
2119:                 process_channel_spectrum_data(spectrum);
2120:             }
2121:         }
2122:     }
2123: }

2138: void DroneHardwareController::process_channel_spectrum_data(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum) {
2139:     MutexLock lock(spectrum_mutex_);
2140: 
2141:     // Copy spectrum data (usually 240 or 256 bins)
2142:     size_t count = std::min(spectrum.db.size(), last_spectrum_db_.size());
2143:     std::copy(spectrum.db.begin(), spectrum.db.begin() + count, last_spectrum_db_.begin());
2144: 
2145:     spectrum_updated_ = true;
2146: }

2170: 
2171: SmartThreatHeader::SmartThreatHeader(Rect parent_rect)
2172:     : View(parent_rect),
2173:       threat_progress_bar_({0, 0, screen_width, 16}),
2174:       threat_status_main_({0, 20, screen_width, 16}, "THREAT: LOW | <0 ~0 >0"),
2175:       threat_frequency_({0, 38, screen_width, 16}, "2400.0MHz SCANNING") {
2176:     last_text_[0] = '\0';
2177:     add_children({&threat_progress_bar_, &threat_status_main_, &threat_frequency_});
2178:     update(ThreatLevel::NONE, 0, 0, 0, 2400000000ULL, false);
2179: }
2180: 
2181: void SmartThreatHeader::update(ThreatLevel max_threat, size_t approaching, size_t static_count,
2182:                                 size_t receding, Frequency current_freq, bool is_scanning) {
2183:     // Check-Before-Update Pattern: Only update if data actually changed
2184:     bool data_changed = (max_threat != last_threat_) ||
2185:                         (is_scanning != last_is_scanning_) ||
2186:                         (current_freq != last_freq_) ||
2187:                         (approaching != last_approaching_) ||
2188:                         (static_count != last_static_) ||
2189:                         (receding != last_receding_);
2190: 
2191:     if (!data_changed) {
2192:         return; // Exit early, no need to redraw
2193:     }
2194: 
2195:     // Update cached values
2196:     last_threat_ = max_threat;
2197:     last_is_scanning_ = is_scanning;
2198:     last_freq_ = current_freq;
2199:     last_approaching_ = approaching;
2200:     last_static_ = static_count;
2201:     last_receding_ = receding;
2202: 
2203:     size_t total_drones = approaching + static_count + receding;
2204:     threat_progress_bar_.set_value(total_drones * 10);
2205: 
2206:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2207:     char buffer[64];
2208:     const char* threat_name = UnifiedStringLookup::threat_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(max_threat));
2209:     if (total_drones > 0) {
2210:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "THREAT: %s | <%lu ~%lu >%lu",
2211:                                   threat_name,
2212:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(approaching),
2213:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(static_count),
2214:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(receding));
2215:     } else if (is_scanning) {
2216:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "SCANNING: <%lu ~%lu >%lu",
2217:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(approaching),
2218:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(static_count),
2219:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(receding));
2220:     } else {
2221:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "READY");
2222:     }
2223:     threat_status_main_.set(buffer);
2224:     threat_status_main_.set_style(&UIStyles::RED_STYLE);
2225:     safe_strcpy(last_text_, buffer, sizeof(last_text_));
2226: 
2227:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use FrequencyFormatter
2228:     if (current_freq > 0) {
2229:         // ?? FIX: Use buffer-based formatting (no std::string allocation)
2230:         char freq_buf[16];
2231:         FrequencyFormatter::to_string_short_freq_buffer(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), current_freq);
2232:         if (is_scanning) {
2233:             StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s SCANNING", freq_buf);
2234:         } else {
2235:             StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s READY", freq_buf);
2236:         }
2237:         threat_frequency_.set(buffer);
2238:     } else {
2239:         threat_frequency_.set("NO SIGNAL");
2240:     }
2241: 
2242:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified color mapping
2243:     static constexpr const Style* const THREAT_STYLES[5] = {
2244:         &UIStyles::LIGHT_STYLE,  // NONE (0)
2245:         &UIStyles::GREEN_STYLE,   // LOW (1)
2246:         &UIStyles::YELLOW_STYLE,  // MEDIUM (2)
2247:         &UIStyles::YELLOW_STYLE,  // HIGH (3)
2248:         &UIStyles::RED_STYLE      // CRITICAL (4)
2249:     };
2250:     uint8_t threat_idx = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(max_threat), static_cast<uint8_t>(4));
2251:     threat_frequency_.set_style(THREAT_STYLES[threat_idx]);
2252:     set_dirty();
2253: }

2257:         update(threat, last_approaching_, last_static_, last_receding_,
2258:                last_freq_, last_is_scanning_);
2259:     }
2260: }

2300: void SmartThreatHeader::paint(Painter& painter) {
2301:     // 1. Fill entire background with threat color
2302:     Color bg_color = UnifiedColorLookup::header_bar(static_cast<uint8_t>(last_threat_));
2303:     painter.fill_rectangle(screen_rect(), bg_color);
2304: 
2305:     // 2. Draw large centered text with white color on colored background
2306:     // Calculate centered position
2307:     const int text_width = strlen(last_text_) * 8; // fixed_8x16 is 8px per char
2308:     const int text_height = 16;
2309:     const int center_x = (screen_width - text_width) / 2;
2310:     const int center_y = (60 - text_height) / 2; // Header height is 60px
2311:     Point text_pos = {center_x, center_y};
2312:     auto style = Style{font::fixed_8x16, bg_color, Color::white()};
2313:     painter.draw_string(text_pos, style, last_text_);

2319:       last_frequency_(0), last_threat_(ThreatLevel::NONE),
2320:       last_trend_(MovementTrend::UNKNOWN), last_rssi_(-120) {
