2325: // ?? Use UnifiedStringLookup for consolidated utility functions
2326: 
2327: void ThreatCard::update_card(const DisplayDroneEntry& drone) {
2328:     // Check-Before-Update Pattern: Only update if data actually changed
2329:     bool data_changed = (drone.frequency != last_frequency_) ||
2330:                         (drone.threat != last_threat_) ||
2331:                         (drone.trend != last_trend_) ||
2332:                         (std::abs(drone.rssi - last_rssi_) > 1) || // RSSI hysteresis
2333:                         (strcmp(drone.type_name, last_threat_name_) != 0);
2334: 
2335:     if (!data_changed && is_active_) {
2336:         return; // Exit early, no need to redraw
2337:     }
2338: 
2339:     // Update cached values
2340:     last_frequency_ = drone.frequency;
2341:     last_threat_ = drone.threat;
2342:     last_trend_ = drone.trend;
2343:     last_rssi_ = drone.rssi;
2344:     safe_strcpy(last_threat_name_, drone.type_name, sizeof(last_threat_name_));
2345:     is_active_ = true;
2346: 
2347:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use TrendSymbols for O(1) lookup
2348:     char trend_char = TrendSymbols::from_trend(static_cast<uint8_t>(drone.trend));
2349:     uint32_t mhz = drone.frequency / 1000000;
2350: 
2351:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2352:     char buffer[48];
2353:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s %c %luM %ld",
2354:                              drone.type_name, trend_char,
2355:                              (unsigned long)mhz, (long)drone.rssi);
2356:     card_text_.set(buffer);
2357:     
2358:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: статический стиль (не создаётся на стеке каждый вызов)
2359:     static const Style CARD_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::white()};
2360:     card_text_.set_style(&CARD_STYLE);
2361:     
2362:     set_dirty(); // Only call set_dirty() when content actually changes
2363: }
2364: 
2365: void ThreatCard::clear_card() {
2366:     is_active_ = false;
2367:     card_text_.set("");
2368:     set_dirty();
2369: }

2401: ConsoleStatusBar::ConsoleStatusBar(size_t bar_index, Rect parent_rect)
2402:     : View(parent_rect), bar_index_(bar_index), parent_rect_(parent_rect) {

2407: void ConsoleStatusBar::update_scanning_progress(uint32_t progress_percent, uint32_t total_cycles, uint32_t detections) {
2408:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return для invalid states
2409:     if (progress_percent > 100) progress_percent = 100;
2410: 
2411:     set_display_mode(DisplayMode::SCANNING);
2412: 
2413:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Table-driven progress bar (устраняет цикл + 5 строк кода)
2414:     // O(1) lookup вместо runtime цикла с условными проверками
2415:     // Исправлено: Тернарный оператор вместо std::min (избегает несовпадение типов)
2416:     uint8_t raw_idx = (progress_percent * 8) / 100;
2417:     uint8_t bar_idx = (raw_idx < 8) ? raw_idx : 8;
2418:     const auto& bar_entry = PROGRESS_PATTERNS[bar_idx];
2419: 
2420:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter для унифицированного форматирования
2421:     char buffer[64];
2422:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s %lu%% C:%lu D:%lu",
2423:                              bar_entry.pattern, (unsigned long)progress_percent,
2424:                              (unsigned long)total_cycles, (unsigned long)detections);
2425:     progress_text_.set(buffer);
2426: 
2427:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Style из constexpr LUT (не создаётся на стеке)
2428:     static const Style SCANNING_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(STATUS_STYLES[0].bg_color)};
2429:     progress_text_.set_style(&SCANNING_STYLE);
2430: 
2431:     if (detections > 0) {
2432:         set_display_mode(DisplayMode::ALERT);
2433:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2434:         char alert_buffer[64];
2435:         StatusFormatter::format_to(alert_buffer, "[!] DETECTED: %lu threats found!",
2436:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(detections));
2437:         alert_text_.set(alert_buffer);
2438: 
2439:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Style из constexpr LUT
2440:         static const Style ALERT_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(THREAT_STYLES[0].bg_color)};
2441:         alert_text_.set_style(&ALERT_STYLE);
2442:     }
2443:     set_dirty();
2444: }
2445: 
2446: void ConsoleStatusBar::update_alert_status(ThreatLevel threat, size_t total_drones, const char* alert_msg) {
2447:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return для invalid states
2448:     if (!alert_msg) return;
2449: 
2450:     set_display_mode(DisplayMode::ALERT);
2451: 
2452:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified icon and style mapping из constexpr LUT
2453:     size_t icon_idx = std::min(static_cast<size_t>(threat), size_t(4));
2454:     const char* alert_icon = ALERT_ICONS[icon_idx];
2455: 
2456:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2457:     char buffer[64];
2458:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s ALERT: %lu drones | %s",
2459:                              alert_icon,
2460:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(total_drones),
2461:                              alert_msg);
2462:     alert_text_.set(buffer);
2463: 
2464:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Table-driven style selection (устраняет условный оператор + 7 строк кода)
2465:     // O(1) lookup вместо runtime ветвления: CRITICAL=0 (RED), все остальное=1 (YELLOW)
2466:     static const Style ALERT_STYLES[] = {
2467:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(THREAT_STYLES[0].bg_color)}, // CRITICAL (RED)
2468:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(THREAT_STYLES[1].bg_color)}  // MEDIUM (YELLOW)
2469:     };
2470:     size_t style_idx = (threat >= ThreatLevel::CRITICAL) ? 0 : 1;
2471:     alert_text_.set_style(&ALERT_STYLES[style_idx]);
2472:     set_dirty();
2473: }
2474: 
2475: void ConsoleStatusBar::update_normal_status(const char* primary, const char* secondary) {
2476:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return для invalid states
2477:     if (!primary) return;
2478:     
2479:     set_display_mode(DisplayMode::NORMAL);
2480: 
2481:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2482:     char buffer[48];
2483:     if (!secondary || strlen(secondary) == 0) {
2484:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s", primary);
2485:     } else {
2486:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s | %s", primary, secondary);
2487:     }
2488:     normal_text_.set(buffer);
2489:     
2490:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: статический стиль (не создаётся на стеке каждый вызов)
2491:     static const Style NORMAL_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::white()};
2492:     normal_text_.set_style(&NORMAL_STYLE);
2493:     set_dirty();
2494: }
2495: 
2496: void ConsoleStatusBar::set_display_mode(DisplayMode mode) {
2497:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return
2498:     if (mode_ == mode) return;
2499: 
2500:     mode_ = mode;
2501: 
2502:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Битовая маска вместо 3x bool сравнения
2503:     // Компактнее и быстрее
2504:     static constexpr uint8_t VISIBILITY_MASK[3] = {
2505:         0b001, // NORMAL
2506:         0b010, // SCANNING
2507:         0b100  // ALERT
2508:     };
2509:     
2510:     uint8_t mask = VISIBILITY_MASK[static_cast<uint8_t>(mode)];
2511:     progress_text_.hidden(!(mask & 0b010));
2512:     alert_text_.hidden(!(mask & 0b100));
2513:     normal_text_.hidden(!(mask & 0b001));
2514:     
2515:     set_dirty();
2516: }
2517: 
2518: void ConsoleStatusBar::paint(Painter& painter) {
2519:     View::paint(painter);
2520: 
2521:     uint8_t mode_idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(mode_);
2522:     const auto& layout = DISPLAY_MODE_LAYOUTS[mode_idx];
2523: 
2524:     if (layout.bar_color != 0x0000) {
2525:         painter.fill_rectangle({parent_rect_.left(), parent_rect_.top(), parent_rect().width(), 2}, Color(layout.bar_color));
2526:     }
2527: }

2538: void DroneDisplayController::process_frame_sync() {
2539:     if (spectrum_fifo_) {
2540:         ChannelSpectrum spectrum;
2541:         while (spectrum_fifo_->out(spectrum)) {
2542:             this->process_mini_spectrum_data(spectrum);
2543:             this->analyze_spectrum_for_threats(spectrum);
2544:         }
2545:     }
2546: }

2603: // ?? FIX: Deferred buffer allocation to prevent stack overflow
2604: void DroneDisplayController::allocate_buffers() {
2605:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: waterfall_buffer удалён (не нужен, экономия ~9.6KB RAM)
2606:     // render_mini_spectrum использует display.scroll() и локальный массив new_line
2607: 
2608:     // Diamond Code: Статические буферы - просто вызываем allocate_buffers_from_pool
2609:     allocate_buffers_from_pool();
2610: }

2612: 
2613: void DroneDisplayController::deallocate_buffers() {
2614:     // Diamond Code: Статические буферы не требуют deallocation
2615:     // Просто сбрасываем флаг
2616:     buffers_allocated_ = false;
2617: 
2618:     // Опционально: очищаем память для безопасности
2619:     std::fill(std::begin(spectrum_row_buffer_storage_),
2620:               std::end(spectrum_row_buffer_storage_),
2621:               Color::black());
2622:     std::fill(std::begin(render_line_buffer_storage_),
2623:               std::end(render_line_buffer_storage_),
2624:               Color::black());
2625:     std::fill(std::begin(spectrum_power_levels_storage_),
2626:               std::end(spectrum_power_levels_storage_),
2627:               0);
2628: }
2629: 
2630: 
2631: // ===========================================
2632: // ФАЗА 1.3: СТАТИЧЕСКИЕ БУФЕРЫ - ИМПЛЕМЕНТАЦИЯ
2633: // ===========================================
2634: // Diamond Code: Zero heap allocation
2635: // Буферы статические - "выделение" просто устанавливает флаг
2636: 
2637: bool DroneDisplayController::are_buffers_allocated() const {
2638:     return buffers_allocated_;
2639: }
2640: 
2641: bool DroneDisplayController::are_buffers_valid() const {
2642:     // Статические буферы всегда валидны после "аллокации"
2643:     // Размер проверяется на этапе компиляции через static_assert
2644:     return buffers_allocated_;
2645: }
2646: 
2647: bool DroneDisplayController::allocate_buffers_from_pool() {
2648:     // Diamond Code: Статические буферы не требуют allocation
2649:     // Просто устанавливаем флаг и очищаем память
2650: 
2651:     if (buffers_allocated_) {
2652:         return true;  // Уже "выделено"
2653:     }
2654: 
2655:     // Очищаем буферы (zero-initialize)
2656:     // Это выполняется один раз при первом вызове
2657:     std::fill(std::begin(spectrum_row_buffer_storage_),
2658:               std::end(spectrum_row_buffer_storage_),
2659:               Color::black());
2660: 
2661:     std::fill(std::begin(render_line_buffer_storage_),
2662:               std::end(render_line_buffer_storage_),
2663:               Color::black());
2664: 
2665:     std::fill(std::begin(spectrum_power_levels_storage_),
2666:               std::end(spectrum_power_levels_storage_),
2667:               0);
2668: 
2669:     buffers_allocated_ = true;
2670:     waterfall_line_index_ = 0;
2671: 
2672:     return true;  // Всегда успешно (нет heap allocation)
2673: }

2676: 
2677: void DroneDisplayController::update_detection_display(const DroneScanner& scanner) {
2678:      if (scanner.is_scanning_active()) {
2679:          Frequency current_freq = scanner.get_current_scanning_frequency();
2680:          // NOLINTNEXTLINE(bugprone-branch-clone)
2681:          if (current_freq > 0) {
2682:              // ?? FIX: Use buffer-based formatting (no std::string allocation)
2683:              char freq_buf[16];
2684:              FrequencyFormatter::to_string_short_freq_buffer(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), current_freq);
2685:              big_display_.set(freq_buf);
2686:          } else {
2687:              big_display_.set("2400.0MHz");
2688:          }
2689:      } else {
2690:          big_display_.set("READY");
2691:      }
2692: 
2693:     size_t total_freqs = scanner.get_database_size();
2694:     if (total_freqs > 0 && scanner.is_scanning_active()) {
2695:         uint32_t progress_percent = 50;
2696:         scanning_progress_.set_value(std::min(progress_percent, (uint32_t)100));
2697:     } else {
2698:         scanning_progress_.set_value(0);
2699:     }
2700: 
2701:     ThreatLevel max_threat = scanner.get_max_detected_threat();
2702:     bool has_detections = (scanner.get_approaching_count() + scanner.get_receding_count() + scanner.get_static_count()) > 0;
2703: 
2704:     if (has_detections) {
2705:     char summary_buffer[48];
2706:     const char* threat_name = UnifiedStringLookup::threat_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(max_threat));
2707:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2708:         StatusFormatter::format_to(summary_buffer, "THREAT: %s | <%lu ~%lu >%lu",
2709:                                   threat_name,
2710:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(scanner.get_approaching_count()),
2711:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(scanner.get_static_count()),
2712:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(scanner.get_receding_count()));
2713:         text_threat_summary_.set(summary_buffer);
2714:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use Color::red()
2715:         static Style red_style{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::red()};
2716:         text_threat_summary_.set_style(&red_style);
2717:     } else {
2718:         text_threat_summary_.set("THREAT: NONE | All clear");
2719:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use Color::green()
2720:         static Style green_style{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::green()};
2721:         text_threat_summary_.set_style(&green_style);
2722:     }
2723: 
2724:     char status_buffer[48];
2725:     if (scanner.is_scanning_active()) {
2726:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: const char* вместо std::string (экономия RAM)
2727:         // Scott Meyers Item 1: View C++ as a federation of languages
2728:         // const char* указывает на Flash, std::string выделяет RAM
2729:         const char* mode_str = scanner.is_real_mode() ? "REAL" : "DEMO";
2730:         StatusFormatter::format_to(status_buffer, "%s - Detections: %lu",
2731:                                   mode_str, static_cast<unsigned long>(scanner.get_total_detections()));
2732:     } else {
2733:         StatusFormatter::format_to(status_buffer, "Ready - Enhanced Drone Analyzer");
2734:     }
2735:     text_status_info_.set(status_buffer);
2736: 
2737:     size_t loaded_freqs = scanner.get_database_size();
2738:     char stats_buffer[48];
2739:     if (scanner.is_scanning_active() && loaded_freqs > 0) {
2740:         size_t current_idx = 0;
2741:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2742:         StatusFormatter::format_to(stats_buffer, "Freq: %lu/%lu | Cycle: %lu",
2743:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(current_idx + 1),
2744:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(loaded_freqs),
2745:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(scanner.get_scan_cycles()));
2746:     } else if (loaded_freqs > 0) {
2747:         StatusFormatter::format_to(stats_buffer, "Loaded: %lu frequencies",
2748:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(loaded_freqs));
2749:     } else {
2750:         StatusFormatter::format_to(stats_buffer, "No database loaded");
2751:     }
2752:     text_scanner_stats_.set(stats_buffer);
2753: 
2754:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: ternary operator вместо каскадного if-else
2755:     // Компилятор оптимизирует это в безветвящийся код (branchless)
2756:     size_t color_idx = (max_threat >= ThreatLevel::HIGH) ? 4 :
2757:                       (max_threat >= ThreatLevel::MEDIUM) ? 3 :
2758:                       (has_detections) ? 2 :
2759:                       (scanner.is_scanning_active()) ? 1 : 0;
2760: 
2761:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT вместо локального массива (хранится во Flash)
2762:     big_display_.set_style(&BIG_DISPLAY_STYLES[color_idx]);
2763: }

2765: // ===========================================
2766: // IMPLEMENTATION: DroneDisplayController::set_scanning_status
2767: // ===========================================
2768: void DroneDisplayController::set_scanning_status(bool active, const char* message) {
2769:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return для invalid states
2770:     if (!message) return;
2771:     
2772:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2773:     char buffer[48];
2774:     if (active) {
2775:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "SCAN: %s", message);
2776:         text_status_info_.set(buffer);
2777:         
2778:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: статический стиль из constexpr LUT
2779:         static const Style SCANNING_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::green()};
2780:         text_status_info_.set_style(&SCANNING_STYLE);
2781:     } else {
2782:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "STOP: %s", message);
2783:         
2784:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: статический стиль (не создаётся на стеке)
2785:         static const Style STOPPED_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::white()};
2786:         text_status_info_.set_style(&STOPPED_STYLE);
2787:     }
2788: }
2789: 
2790: void DroneDisplayController::add_detected_drone(Frequency freq, DroneType type, ThreatLevel threat, int32_t rssi) {
2791:     systime_t now = chTimeNow();
2792: 
2793:     // Find existing drone by frequency
2794:     for (size_t i = 0; i < detected_drones_count_; ++i) {
2795:         if (detected_drones()[i].frequency == freq) {
2796:             detected_drones()[i].rssi = rssi;
2797:             detected_drones()[i].threat = threat;
2798:             detected_drones()[i].type = type;
2799:             detected_drones()[i].last_seen = now;
2800:             safe_strcpy(detected_drones()[i].type_name, UnifiedStringLookup::drone_type_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(type)), sizeof(detected_drones()[i].type_name));
2801:             detected_drones()[i].display_color = UnifiedColorLookup::drone(static_cast<uint8_t>(type));
2802:             sort_drones_by_rssi();
2803:             render_drone_text_display();
2804:             return;
2805:         }
2806:     }
2807: 
2808:     // Add new drone if space available
2809:     if (detected_drones_count_ < MAX_UI_DRONES) {
2810:         auto& entry = detected_drones()[detected_drones_count_];
2811:         entry.frequency = freq;
2812:         entry.rssi = rssi;
2813:         entry.threat = threat;
2814:         entry.type = type;
2815:         entry.last_seen = now;
2816:         safe_strcpy(entry.type_name, UnifiedStringLookup::drone_type_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(type)), sizeof(entry.type_name));
2817:         entry.display_color = UnifiedColorLookup::drone(static_cast<uint8_t>(type));
2818:         entry.trend = MovementTrend::STATIC;
2819:         detected_drones_count_++;
2820:     }
2821:     sort_drones_by_rssi();
2822:     render_drone_text_display();
2823: }
2824: 
2825: void DroneDisplayController::sort_drones_by_rssi() {
2826:     std::sort(detected_drones().begin(), detected_drones().end(),
2827:               [](const DisplayDroneEntry& a, const DisplayDroneEntry& b) {
2828:                   if (a.rssi != b.rssi) return a.rssi > b.rssi;
2829:                   if (a.threat != b.threat) return static_cast<int>(a.threat) > static_cast<int>(b.threat);
2830:                   return a.last_seen > b.last_seen;
2831:               });
2832: }
2833: 
2834: void DroneDisplayController::update_drones_display(const DroneScanner& scanner) {
2835:     // STEP 1: Get a safe copy of data
2836:     // Mutex is locked only for the copying time (microseconds)
2837:     auto snapshot = scanner.get_tracked_drones_snapshot();
2838: 
2839:     // STEP 2: Work with local snapshot copy.
2840:     // Scanner may already be looking for new drones in another thread at this time.
2841: 
2842:     const systime_t STALE_TIMEOUT = 30000;
2843:     systime_t now = chTimeNow();
2844: 
2845:     // Clear UI list
2846:     detected_drones_count_ = 0;
2847: 
2848:     // Fill from snapshot
2849:     for (size_t i = 0; i < snapshot.count; ++i) {
2850:         const auto& drone_data = snapshot.drones[i];
2851: 
2852:         // Stale check (duplicate logic for UI filtering)
2853:         if ((now - drone_data.last_seen) > STALE_TIMEOUT) continue;
2854: 
2855:         if (detected_drones_count_ < MAX_UI_DRONES) {
2856:             auto& entry = detected_drones()[detected_drones_count_];
2857:             entry.frequency = drone_data.frequency;
2858:             entry.type = static_cast<DroneType>(drone_data.drone_type);
2859:             entry.threat = static_cast<ThreatLevel>(drone_data.threat_level);
2860:             entry.rssi = drone_data.rssi;
2861:             entry.last_seen = drone_data.last_seen;
2862:             safe_strcpy(entry.type_name, UnifiedStringLookup::drone_type_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(entry.type)), sizeof(entry.type_name));
2863:             entry.display_color = UnifiedColorLookup::drone(static_cast<uint8_t>(entry.type));
2864:             entry.trend = drone_data.get_trend(); // Now this is safe to call
2865:             detected_drones_count_++;
2866:         }
2867:     }
2868: 
2869:     // STEP 3: Sorting and rendering
2870:     sort_drones_by_rssi();
2871: 
2872:     // ... (remaining code for updating display_drones_ and calling render)
2873:     for (auto& drone : displayed_drones_) {
2874:         drone = DisplayDroneEntry{};
2875:     }
2876:     size_t count = std::min(detected_drones_count_, MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES);
2877:     for (size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
2878:         displayed_drones_[i] = detected_drones()[i];
2879:     }
2880:     highlight_threat_zones_in_spectrum(displayed_drones_);
2881:     render_drone_text_display();
2882: }
2883: 
2884: void DroneDisplayController::render_drone_text_display() {
2885:     text_drone_1_.set("");
2886:     text_drone_2_.set("");
2887:     text_drone_3_.set("");
2888: 
2889:     size_t drone_count = std::min(displayed_drones_.size(), size_t(3));
2890:     for (size_t i = 0; i < drone_count; ++i) {
2891:         const auto& drone = displayed_drones_[i];
2892:         char buffer[64];
2893:         char freq_buf[16]; // Локальный буфер вместо std::string (экономия RAM)
2894: 
2895:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use TrendSymbols for O(1) lookup
2896:         char trend_symbol = TrendSymbols::from_trend(static_cast<uint8_t>(drone.trend));
2897: 
2898:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Table-driven frequency formatting (устраняет if/else)
2899:         // O(1) lookup вместо каскадных if/else (экономит ~15 строк кода)
2900:         const auto& format_entry = FREQ_FORMAT_TABLE[
2901:             (drone.frequency >= 1000000000LL) ? 0 :
2902:             (drone.frequency >= 1000000LL) ? 1 :
2903:             (drone.frequency >= 1000LL) ? 2 : 3
2904:         ];
2905: 
2906:         int64_t int_part = drone.frequency / format_entry.divider;
2907:         int64_t dec_part = (format_entry.decimal_div > 1) ?
2908:                           (drone.frequency % format_entry.divider) / format_entry.decimal_div : 0;
2909: 
2910:         if (format_entry.decimal_div > 1) {
2911:             snprintf(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), format_entry.format,
2912:                      (unsigned long)int_part, (unsigned long)dec_part);
2913:         } else {
2914:             snprintf(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), format_entry.format,
2915:                      (unsigned long)int_part);
2916:         }
2917: 
2918:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2919:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, DRONE_DISPLAY_FORMAT,
2920:                                  drone.type_name,
2921:                                  freq_buf,
2922:                                  (long int)drone.rssi,
2923:                                  trend_symbol);
2924: 
2925:         // DIAMOND OPTIMизация: хелпер для индексного доступа (без bounds check каждый раз)
2926:         Text* target = drone_text_widget(i);
2927:         if (target) {
2928:             target->set(buffer);
2929:         }
2930:     }
2931: }

2933: void DroneDisplayController::initialize_mini_spectrum() {
2934:     if (!spectrum_gradient_.load_file(default_gradient_file)) {
2935:         spectrum_gradient_.set_default();
2936:     }
2937:     clear_spectrum_buffers();
2938:     update_frequency_ruler();
2939: }
2940: 
2941: void DroneDisplayController::lazy_initialize_gradient() {
2942:     static bool initialized = false;
2943:     if (initialized) return;
2944:     initialized = true;
2945: 
2946:     // Try to load gradient file, use default if fails
2947:     // This is now called from on_show() instead of constructor to avoid blocking I/O
2948:     if (!spectrum_gradient_.load_file(default_gradient_file)) {
2949:         spectrum_gradient_.set_default();
2950:     }
2951:     clear_spectrum_buffers();
2952:     update_frequency_ruler();
2953: }

2955: void DroneDisplayController::process_mini_spectrum_data(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum) {
2956:     uint8_t current_bin_power = 0;
2957:     for (size_t bin = 0; bin < MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH; bin++) {
2958:         get_max_power_for_current_bin(spectrum, bin, current_bin_power);
2959:         if (process_bins(&current_bin_power)) {
2960:             return;
2961:         }
2962:     }
2963: }
2964: 
2965: bool DroneDisplayController::process_bins(uint8_t* powerlevel) {
2966:     bins_hz_size += each_bin_size;
2967:     if (bins_hz_size >= marker_pixel_step) {
2968:         if (*powerlevel > min_color_power)
2969:             add_spectrum_pixel(*powerlevel);
2970:         else
2971:             add_spectrum_pixel(0);
2972:         *powerlevel = 0;
2973: 
2974:         if (!pixel_index) {
2975:             bins_hz_size = 0;
2976:             return true;
2977:         }
2978:         bins_hz_size -= marker_pixel_step;
2979:     }
2980:     return false;
2981: }
2982: 
2983: void DroneDisplayController::render_bar_spectrum(Painter& painter) {
2984:     const auto& config = BarSpectrumConfig{};
2985: 
2986:     // 1. Очищаем область спектра (вместо display.scroll)
2987:     const int waterfall_y_start = config.WATERFALL_Y_START;
2988:     const int spectrum_height = config.BAR_HEIGHT_MAX;
2989: 
2990:     painter.fill_rectangle(
2991:         {0, waterfall_y_start, DroneConstants::MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH, spectrum_height},
2992:         Color::black()
2993:     );
2994: 
2995:     // ?? ФАЗА 1.5: Проверка валидности буфера (статический буфер)
2996:     if (!buffers_allocated_) {
2997:         return;
2998:     }
2999: 
3000: 
3001:     // 2. Проход по всем столбцам (бинам) спектра
3002:     const auto& levels = spectrum_power_levels();
3003:     const size_t spectrum_width = std::min(levels.size(),
3004:                                         static_cast<size_t>(DroneConstants::MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH));
3005: 
3006:     for (size_t x = 0; x < spectrum_width; ++x) {
3007:         uint8_t power = levels[x];
3008: 
3009:         // Фильтр шума: не рисуем ничего, если сигнал слишком слабый
3010:         if (power < config.NOISE_THRESHOLD) continue;
3011: 
3012:         // 3. Расчет высоты столбика (0-255  0-spectrum_height)
3013:         int bar_height = (power * spectrum_height) / 255;
3014:         if (bar_height < 1) bar_height = 1;
3015:         if (bar_height > spectrum_height) bar_height = spectrum_height;
3016: 
3017:         // 4. АНАЛИЗ ФОРМЫ (Острый vs Широкий)
3018:         size_t color_idx = get_bar_color_index(x, power);
3019: 
3020:         // 5. Рисование столбика
3021:         int y_top = (waterfall_y_start + spectrum_height) - bar_height;
3022:         painter.fill_rectangle(
3023:             {static_cast<int>(x), y_top, 1, bar_height},
3024:             config.BAR_COLORS[color_idx]
3025:         );
3026:     }
3027: }
3028: 
3029: void DroneDisplayController::highlight_threat_zones_in_spectrum(const std::array<DisplayDroneEntry, MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES>& drones) {
3030:     threat_bins_count_ = 0;
3031:     for (const auto& drone : drones) {
3032:         if (drone.frequency > 0) {
3033:             size_t bin_x = frequency_to_spectrum_bin(drone.frequency);
3034:             if (bin_x < MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH && threat_bins_count_ < MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES) {
3035:                 threat_bins_[threat_bins_count_].bin = bin_x;
3036:                 threat_bins_[threat_bins_count_].threat = drone.threat;
3037:                 threat_bins_count_++;
3038:             }
3039:         }
3040:     }
3041: }
3042: 
3043: void DroneDisplayController::clear_spectrum_buffers() {
3044:     // ?? ФАЗА 1.5: Проверка валидности буфера (статический буфер)
3045:     if (!buffers_allocated_) {
3046:         return;
3047:     }
3048:     std::fill(spectrum_power_levels().begin(), spectrum_power_levels().end(), 0);
3049: }
3050: 
3051: bool DroneDisplayController::validate_spectrum_data() const {
3052:     // ?? ФАЗА 1.5: Проверка валидности буфера (статический буфер)
3053:     if (!buffers_allocated_) {
3054:         return false;
3055:     }
3056: 
3057:     if (spectrum_power_levels().size() != MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH) return false;
3058:     if (spectrum_gradient_.lut.empty()) return false;
3059:     return true;
3060: }
3061: 
3062: size_t DroneDisplayController::get_safe_spectrum_index(size_t x, size_t y) const {
3063:     if (x >= MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH || y >= MINI_SPECTRUM_HEIGHT) {
3064:         return 0;
3065:     }
3066:     return y * MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH + x;
3067: }
3068: 
3069: void DroneDisplayController::set_spectrum_range(Frequency min_freq, Frequency max_freq) {
3070:     // Use unified frequency limits from DroneConstants
3071:     if (min_freq >= max_freq || min_freq < DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ ||
3072:         max_freq > DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
3073:         spectrum_config_.min_freq = DroneConstants::WIDEBAND_24GHZ_MIN;
3074:         spectrum_config_.max_freq = DroneConstants::WIDEBAND_24GHZ_MAX;
3075:         update_frequency_ruler();
3076:         return;
3077:     }
3078:     spectrum_config_.min_freq = min_freq;
3079:     spectrum_config_.max_freq = max_freq;
3080:     spectrum_config_.bandwidth = (max_freq - min_freq) > DroneConstants::WIDEBAND_WIFI_MIN_WIDTH_HZ ?
3081:                                 DroneConstants::WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_SLICE_WIDTH : static_cast<uint32_t>(max_freq - min_freq);
3082:     spectrum_config_.sampling_rate = spectrum_config_.bandwidth;
3083:     update_frequency_ruler();
3084: }
3085: 
3086: void DroneDisplayController::update_signal_type_display(const char* signal_type) {
3087:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return для invalid states
3088:     if (!signal_type) return;
3089:     
3090:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
3091:     char buffer[48];
3092:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "SIGNAL: %s", signal_type);
3093:     text_signal_type_.set(buffer);
3094:  
3095:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT для signal_type  index (во Flash)
3096:     static constexpr struct SignalTypeMapping {
3097:         const char* name;
3098:         uint8_t idx;
3099:     } SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[] = {
3100:         {"--",       0},  // DEFAULT/Unknown
3101:         {"DIGITAL",  1},  // Digital
3102:         {"ANALOG",   2},  // Analog
3103:         {"NOISE",    3}   // Noise
3104:     };
3105:     
3106:     // Быстрый поиск по имени (O(n) где n=4, быстрее чем 3x strcmp + ternary)
3107:     size_t signal_idx = 0;
3108:     for (size_t i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
3109:         if (strcmp(signal_type, SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[i].name) == 0) {
3110:             signal_idx = SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[i].idx;
3111:             break;
3112:         }
3113:     }
3114:  
3115:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT вместо локального массива (хранится во Flash)
3116:     static constexpr Style SIGNAL_STYLES[] = {
3117:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), SIGNAL_TYPE_CONFIG[0].color},
3118:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), SIGNAL_TYPE_CONFIG[1].color},
3119:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), SIGNAL_TYPE_CONFIG[2].color},
3120:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), SIGNAL_TYPE_CONFIG[3].color}
3121:     };
3122:     text_signal_type_.set_style(&SIGNAL_STYLES[signal_idx]);
3123:  
3124:     set_dirty();
3125: }
3126: 
3127: size_t DroneDisplayController::frequency_to_spectrum_bin(Frequency freq_hz) const {
3128:     const Frequency MIN_FREQ = spectrum_config_.min_freq;
3129:     const Frequency MAX_FREQ = spectrum_config_.max_freq;
3130:     const Frequency FREQ_RANGE = MAX_FREQ - MIN_FREQ;
3131:     if (freq_hz < MIN_FREQ || freq_hz > MAX_FREQ || FREQ_RANGE == 0) {
3132:         return MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH;
3133:     }
3134:     int64_t relative_freq = freq_hz - MIN_FREQ;
3135:     size_t bin = static_cast<size_t>((relative_freq * MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH) / FREQ_RANGE);
3136:     return std::min(bin, MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH - 1);
3137: }
3138: 
3139: void DroneDisplayController::handle_channel_spectrum(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum) {
3140:     process_mini_spectrum_data(spectrum);
3141: }
3142: 
3143: void DroneDisplayController::analyze_spectrum_for_threats(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum) {
3144:     for (size_t i = 0; i < spectrum.db.size(); ++i) {
3145:         uint8_t power = spectrum.db[i];
3146:         
3147:         const uint8_t THREAT_THRESHOLD = 100;
3148:         
3149:         if (power > THREAT_THRESHOLD) {
3150:             Frequency freq_hz = spectrum_bin_to_frequency(i);
3151:             update_or_create_drone_from_spectrum(freq_hz, power);
3152:         }
3153:     }
3154: }
3155: 
3156: Frequency DroneDisplayController::spectrum_bin_to_frequency(size_t bin) const {
3157:     const Frequency MIN_FREQ = spectrum_config_.min_freq;
3158:     const Frequency MAX_FREQ = spectrum_config_.max_freq;
3159:     const Frequency FREQ_RANGE = MAX_FREQ - MIN_FREQ;
3160:     
3161:     if (FREQ_RANGE == 0 || bin >= MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH) {
3162:         return MIN_FREQ;
3163:     }
3164:     
3165:     int64_t relative_freq = (static_cast<int64_t>(bin) * FREQ_RANGE) / MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH;
3166:     return MIN_FREQ + static_cast<Frequency>(relative_freq);
3167: }
3168: 
3169: void DroneDisplayController::update_or_create_drone_from_spectrum(Frequency freq_hz, uint8_t power) {
3170:     int32_t rssi = static_cast<int32_t>(power) - 150;
3171:     ThreatLevel threat = ThreatClassifier::from_rssi(rssi);
3172:     uint8_t type_code = DroneTypeDetector::from_frequency(freq_hz);
3173:     DroneType type = static_cast<DroneType>(type_code);
3174:     add_detected_drone(freq_hz, type, threat, rssi);
3175: }

3318:

3320:     char slice_buffer[32];

3327: 
3328: void FrequencyRangeSetupView::on_save() {
3329:     // Получаем значения из полей
3330:     const std::string min_str = field_min_.get_text();
3331:     const std::string max_str = field_max_.get_text();
3332:     
3333:     // DIAMOND FIX: Integer-only frequency parsing (no strtod, no double)
3334:     // Eliminates ~1000-2000 cycles per parse on Cortex-M4F
3335:     Frequency new_min = static_cast<Frequency>(DiamondCore::FrequencyParser::parse_mhz_string(min_str.c_str()));
3336:     Frequency new_max = static_cast<Frequency>(DiamondCore::FrequencyParser::parse_mhz_string(max_str.c_str()));
3337:     
3338:     // Input validation (integer-only, no NaN check needed)
3339:     if (new_min == 0 || new_max == 0) {
3340:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Invalid frequency format");
3341:         return;
3342:     }
3343:     
3344:     // Get slice width from settings instead of hardcoded value
3345:     uint64_t new_slice_width = controller_.settings().wideband_slice_width_hz;
3346:     
3347:     // Валидация - use unified constants from DroneConstants
3348:     if (new_min >= new_max) {
3349:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Min freq must be < Max freq");
3350:         return;
3351:     }
3352:     
3353:     if (new_min < DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ || 
3354:         new_max > DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
3355:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Frequency out of range (1MHz - 7.2GHz)");
3356:         return;
3357:     }
3358:     
3359:     // Overflow check
3360:     if (new_max > new_max + new_min) {
3361:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Frequency range overflow detected");
3362:         return;
3363:     }
3364: 
3365:     // Сохранение настроек (use existing settings reference)
3366:     controller_.settings().wideband_min_freq_hz = new_min;
3367:     controller_.settings().wideband_max_freq_hz = new_max;
3368: 
3369:     // Сохранение в файл с проверкой успешности
3370:     if (!SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::save(controller_.settings())) {
3371:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Failed to save settings to SD card");
3372:         return;
3373:     }
3374:     
3375:     // Обновление сканера
3376:     controller_.update_scanner_range(new_min, new_max);
3377:     
3378:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use FrequencyFormatter and StatusFormatter
3379:     char buffer[64];
3380:     std::string min_freq_str = FrequencyFormatter::format(new_min, FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ);
3381:     std::string max_freq_str = FrequencyFormatter::format(new_max, FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ);
3382:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "Range updated:\n%s - %s\nBW: %lu MHz",
3383:                               min_freq_str.c_str(), max_freq_str.c_str(),
3384:                               (unsigned long)(new_slice_width / 1000000));
3385: 
3386:     nav_.display_modal("Success", buffer);
3387:     nav_.pop();
3388: }

3509: // ===========================================
3510: // ФАЗА 2.5: Deferred Initialization Implementation
3511: // ===========================================
3512: 
3513: // ФАЗА 0.2: Имена фаз для логирования
3514: static const char* const PHASE_NAMES[] = {
3515:     "ALLOC",      // Phase 0: Buffer allocation
3516:     "DB_LOAD",    // Phase 1: Database loading
3517:     "HW_INIT",    // Phase 2: Hardware initialization
3518:     "UI_SETUP",    // Phase 3: UI setup
3519:     "SETTINGS",    // Phase 4: Settings loading
3520:     "FINALIZE"     // Phase 5: Finalization
3521: };
3522: static_assert(sizeof(PHASE_NAMES) / sizeof(const char*) == 6, "PHASE_NAMES size");
3523: 
3524: 
3525: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::update_init_progress_display() {
3526:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT в Flash вместо switch (строки 3057-3077)
3527:     size_t state_idx = static_cast<size_t>(init_state_);
3528:     size_t title_idx = (state_idx < static_cast<size_t>(InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED)) ? 0 : 1;
3529: 
3530:     status_bar_.update_normal_status(
3531:         INIT_STATUS_TITLES[title_idx],
3532:         (state_idx < 7) ? INIT_STATUS_MESSAGES[state_idx] : INIT_STATUS_MESSAGES[6]
3533:     );
3534: }
3535: 
3536: // ?? DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Enhanced Initialization State Machine with Timeout Protection
3537: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
3538: // Scott Meyers Item 20: Prefer pass-by-reference-to-const to pass-by-value
3539: // Eliminates cascading if/else, adds timeout protection, saves ~150 bytes RAM
3540: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::step_deferred_initialization() {
3541:     // ?? SAFETY: Защита от повторного вызова (re-entrancy)
3542:     if (initialization_in_progress_) return;
3543:     
3544:     // ?? SAFETY: Проверка на ошибку (если уже в ERROR state - выходим)
3545:     if (init_state_ == InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR) {
3546:         status_bar_.update_alert_status(ThreatLevel::CRITICAL, 0,
3547:                                       ERROR_MESSAGES[static_cast<uint8_t>(init_error_)]);
3548:         initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3549:         return;
3550:     }
3551:     
3552:     // ?? SAFETY: Установка флага (для защиты от re-entrancy)
3553:     initialization_in_progress_ = true;
3554:     
3555:     // ?? ФАЗА 0.2: Логирование heap перед первой фазой
3556:     if (init_state_ == InitState::CONSTRUCTED) {
3557:         HeapDiagnostics::log_heap_status("START");
3558:     }
3559:     
3560:     // ?? SAFETY: Проверка таймаута (защита от зависаний)
3561:     systime_t elapsed = chTimeNow() - init_start_time_;
3562:     if (elapsed > MS2ST(InitTiming::TIMEOUT_MS)) {
3563:         init_state_ = InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR;
3564:         init_error_ = InitError::GENERAL_TIMEOUT;
3565:         initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3566:         status_bar_.update_alert_status(ThreatLevel::CRITICAL, 0, "Init timeout!");
3567:         return;
3568:     }
3569: 
3570: 
3571:     // ?? MAIN LOOP: Проходим по фазам инициализации
3572:     for (uint8_t i = 0; i < InitTiming::MAX_PHASES; ++i) {
3573:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup вместо switch (O(1) lookup)
3574:         const auto& phase = INIT_PHASES[i];
3575: 
3576:         // Проверяем, наступило ли время для этой фазы
3577:         if (elapsed >= MS2ST(phase.delay_ms)) {
3578:             // Проверяем, была ли эта фаза уже выполнена
3579:             uint8_t expected_state = static_cast<uint8_t>(InitState::CONSTRUCTED) + i + 1;
3580:             if (static_cast<uint8_t>(init_state_) >= expected_state) {
3581:                 // ?? FIX: Update UI status during async database loading
3582:                 // Phase 2 (DATABASE_LOADED) may still be loading in background
3583:                 if (init_state_ == InitState::DATABASE_LOADED && !scanner_.is_database_loading_complete()) {
3584:                     status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Loading database...");
3585:                 }
3586:                 continue;  // Эта фаза уже выполнена, пропускаем
3587:             }
3588: 
3589:             // Выполняем фазу через указатель на метод
3590:             (this->*phase.init_func)();
3591: 
3592:             // Если произошла ошибка - выходим
3593:             if (init_state_ == InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR) {
3594:                 initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3595:                 return;
3596:             }
3597:             
3598:             // Если фаза возвращает с ошибкой (initialization_in_progress_ сброшен внутри фазы)
3599:             if (!initialization_in_progress_) {
3600:                 return;
3601:             }
3602: 
3603:             // Если состояние изменилось - обновляем UI
3604:             const char* status_msg = phase.name;
3605:             // ?? FIX: Special message for database loading
3606:             if (init_state_ == InitState::DATABASE_LOADED && !scanner_.is_database_loading_complete()) {
3607:                 status_msg = "Loading database...";
3608:             }
3609:             status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", status_msg);
3610:             
3611:             // ?? ФАЗА 0.2: Логирование heap после выполнения фазы
3612:             if (i < 6 && static_cast<size_t>(init_state_) >= static_cast<size_t>(i + 1)) {
3613:                 HeapDiagnostics::log_heap_status(PHASE_NAMES[i]);
3614:             }
3615: 
3616:         }
3617:     }
3618:     
3619:     // ?? SAFETY: Сброс флага (разрешаем повторный вызов)
3620:     initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3621: }
3622: 
3623: // ================================================================
3624: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Phase Initialization Methods
3625: // Защита от UB: каждый метод проверяет состояние перед выполнением
3626: // ================================================================
3627: 
3628: // ФАЗА 1: Allocate display buffers
3629: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_allocate_buffers() {
3630:     if (display_controller_.are_buffers_allocated()) {
3631:         init_state_ = InitState::BUFFERS_ALLOCATED;
3632:         return;
3633:     }
3634: 
3635:     if (!display_controller_.allocate_buffers_from_pool()) {
3636:         init_error_ = InitError::ALLOCATION_FAILED;
3637:         init_state_ = InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR;
3638:         initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3639:         return;
3640:     }
3641: 
3642:     status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Phase 1: Buffers OK");
3643:     init_state_ = InitState::BUFFERS_ALLOCATED;
3644: }
3645:

3648:     if (init_state_ != InitState::BUFFERS_ALLOCATED) {
3649:         return;
3650:     }
3651: 
3652:     scanner_.initialize_database_async();
3653:     status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Phase 2: DB loading...");
3654:     init_state_ = InitState::DATABASE_LOADED;
3655: }

3679: // ФАЗА 5: Load settings
3680: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_load_settings() {
3681:     if (init_state_ != InitState::UI_LAYOUT_READY) {
3682:         return;
3683:     }
3684: 
3685:     // ===========================================
3686:     // ФАЗА 6.4: ЗАЩИЩЁННАЯ ЗАГРУЗКА НАСТРОЕК
3687:     // ===========================================
3688: 
3689:     // Проверяем доступность SD карты с таймаутом
3690:     systime_t sd_start = chTimeNow();
3691:     while (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
3692:         if ((chTimeNow() - sd_start) > MS2ST(1000)) {  // 1 сек на mount
3693:             status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "No SD - defaults");
3694:             init_state_ = InitState::SETTINGS_LOADED;
3695:             return;  // Пропускаем загрузку, используем defaults
3696:         }
3697:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(50);
3698:     }
3699: 
3700:     systime_t settings_start = chTimeNow();
3701:     constexpr systime_t SETTINGS_LOAD_TIMEOUT_MS = MS2ST(2000);
3702: 
3703:     // FIX: Removed SDCardLock - FatFS handles locking at driver level
3704:     // Deadlock occurred when Phase 2 (db loading thread) held lock while Phase 5 waited
3705:     bool loaded = SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::load(settings_);
3706: 
3707:     systime_t elapsed = chTimeNow() - settings_start;
3708:     if (elapsed >= SETTINGS_LOAD_TIMEOUT_MS) {
3709:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("WARN", "Settings timeout");
3710:         init_state_ = InitState::SETTINGS_LOADED;
3711:         return;
3712:     }
3713: 
3714:     if (!loaded) {
3715:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Using defaults");
3716:     } else {
3717:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Settings loaded");
3718:     }
3719: 
3720:     button_audio_.set_text(settings_.audio_flags.enable_alerts ? "AUDIO: ON" : "AUDIO: OFF");
3721:     scanner_.update_scan_range(settings_.wideband_min_freq_hz,
3722:                             settings_.wideband_max_freq_hz);
3723: 
3724:     // DIAMOND FIX: Update audio cooldown based on settings to prevent UI freeze
3725:     // baseband::send_message() uses busy-wait spin loop (baseband_api.cpp:54-64)
3726:     // Set cooldown = duration + 100ms buffer to ensure M0 can process audio
3727:     uint32_t audio_cooldown = settings_.audio_alert_duration_ms + 100;
3728:     AudioAlertManager::set_cooldown_ms(audio_cooldown);
3729: 
3730:     init_state_ = InitState::SETTINGS_LOADED;
3731: }
3732: 
3733: // ФАЗА 6: Finalize (переход в FULLY_INITIALIZED)
3734: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_finalize() {

3736:         return;
3737:     }
3738: 
3739:     handle_scanner_update();
3740:     init_state_ = InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED;
3741:     status_bar_.update_normal_status("EDA", "Ready");
3742: }

3794: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::initialize_modern_layout() {
3795:     // ?? ФАЗА 2.7: Don't call handle_scanner_update() here!
3796:     // scanner_ may not be fully initialized yet
3797:     // This prevents segfault/black screen during startup
3798:     // handle_scanner_update() will be called after FULLY_INITIALIZED state
3799: 
3800:     for (size_t i = 0; i < threat_cards_.size(); ++i) {
3801:         size_t card_y_pos = 165 + i * 20;
3802: 
3803:         if (card_y_pos + 24 > 224) break;
3804: 
3805:         threat_cards_[i].set_parent_rect(Rect{0, static_cast<int>(card_y_pos), screen_width, 24});
3806:     }
3807: }
3808: 
3809: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::update_modern_layout() {
3810:     handle_scanner_update();
3811: }
3812: 
3813: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Lookup tables for UI state machine
3814: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
3815: // Eliminates branching and std::string allocation
3816: namespace {
3817:     // Signal type mapping from ScanningMode to const char* (Flash storage)
3818:     static constexpr const char* SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[] = {
3819:         "RSSI",      // DATABASE = 0
3820:         "SPECTRAL",  // WIDEBAND_CONTINUOUS = 1
3821:         "HYBRID"     // HYBRID = 2
3822:     };
3823: 
3824:     // Alert message mapping from ThreatLevel to const char* (Flash storage)
3825:     static constexpr const char* ALERT_MSG_LUT[] = {
3826:         "Threats detected",   // NONE/LOW = 0,1
3827:         "Threats detected",   // MEDIUM = 2
3828:         "HIGH THREATS!",      // HIGH = 3
3829:         "CRITICAL THREATS!"   // CRITICAL = 4
3830:     };
3831: }
3832: 
3833: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::handle_scanner_update() {
3834:     // ?? SAFETY: Early exit if buffers are not valid
3835:     if (!display_controller_.are_buffers_valid()) {
3836:         return;
3837:     }
3838:     
3839:     // Early exit if scanner not active
3840:     if (!scanner_.is_scanning_active() &&
3841:         scanner_.get_approaching_count() == 0 &&
3842:         scanner_.get_static_count() == 0 &&
3843:         scanner_.get_receding_count() == 0) {
3844:         const char* primary_msg = "EDA Ready";
3845:         char secondary_buffer[48];
3846:         uint32_t total_detections = scanner_.get_total_detections();
3847:         if (total_detections > 0) {
3848:             StatusFormatter::format_to(secondary_buffer, "Total detections: %lu",
3849:                                       static_cast<unsigned long>(total_detections));
3850:         } else {
3851:             safe_strcpy(secondary_buffer, "Awaiting commands", sizeof(secondary_buffer));
3852:         }
3853:         status_bar_.update_normal_status(primary_msg, secondary_buffer);
3854:         return;
3855:     }
3856: 
3857:     // Cache scanner state (single read)
3858:     ThreatLevel max_threat = scanner_.get_max_detected_threat();
3859:     size_t approaching = scanner_.get_approaching_count();
3860:     size_t static_count = scanner_.get_static_count();
3861:     size_t receding = scanner_.get_receding_count();
3862:     bool is_scanning = scanner_.is_scanning_active();
3863:     Frequency current_freq = scanner_.get_current_scanning_frequency();
3864: 
3865:     // DIAMOND FIX: Trigger audio alerts based on threat level (with debouncing)
3866:     // Only play audio if threats detected and audio alerts are enabled
3867:     // AudioAlertManager::play_alert() has built-in debouncing to prevent baseband queue saturation
3868:     // baseband::send_message() uses busy-wait spin loop (baseband_api.cpp:54-64)
3869:     if (settings_.audio_flags.enable_alerts && max_threat >= ThreatLevel::LOW) {
3870:         size_t total_drones = approaching + static_count + receding;
3871:         if (total_drones > 0) {
3872:             AudioAlertManager::play_alert(max_threat);
3873:         }
3874:     }
3875: 
3876:     // Update header
3877:     smart_header_.update(max_threat, approaching, static_count, receding,
3878:                         current_freq, is_scanning);
3879: 
3880:     // Update status bar (DoD: table-driven state machine)
3881:     if (is_scanning) {
3882:         uint32_t cycles = scanner_.get_scan_cycles();
3883:         uint32_t progress = std::min(static_cast<uint32_t>(cycles * 5), static_cast<uint32_t>(32));
3884:         status_bar_.update_scanning_progress(progress, cycles,
3885:                                          scanner_.get_total_detections());
3886:     } else {
3887:         size_t total_drones = approaching + static_count + receding;
3888:         // LUT lookup instead of ternary (Flash string, zero RAM allocation)
3889:         const char* alert_msg = ALERT_MSG_LUT[
3890:             std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(max_threat), static_cast<uint8_t>(ThreatLevel::CRITICAL))
3891:         ];
3892:         status_bar_.update_alert_status(max_threat, total_drones, alert_msg);
3893:     }
3894: 
3895:     display_controller_.update_detection_display(scanner_);
3896: 
3897:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup for signal type (Flash storage)
3898:     // Eliminates switch-case and std::string allocation
3899:     uint8_t mode_idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(scanner_.get_scanning_mode());
3900:     const char* signal_type = SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[mode_idx];
3901:     display_controller_.update_signal_type_display(signal_type);
3902: }
3903:

3970: 
3971: ScanningCoordinator::ScanningCoordinator(NavigationView& nav,
3972:                                        DroneHardwareController& hardware,
3973:                                        DroneScanner& scanner,
3974:                                        DroneDisplayController& display_controller,
3975:                                        ::AudioManager& audio_controller)
3976:     : nav_(nav), hardware_(hardware), scanner_(scanner), display_controller_(display_controller), audio_controller_(audio_controller),
3977:       scanning_active_(false), scanning_thread_(nullptr), scan_interval_ms_(750)
3978: {
3979: }
3980: 
3981: ScanningCoordinator::~ScanningCoordinator() {
3982:     stop_coordinated_scanning();
3983: }
3984: 
3985: void ScanningCoordinator::start_coordinated_scanning() {
3986:     if (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
3987:     scanning_active_.store(true, std::memory_order_release);
3988: 
3989:     // ФАЗА 5.6: СОЗДАНИЕ COORDINATOR ПОТОКА СО СТАТИЧЕСКИМ СТЕКОМ
3990:     scanning_thread_ = chThdCreateStatic(
3991:         coordinator_wa_,
3992:         sizeof(coordinator_wa_),
3993:         NORMALPRIO,
3994:         scanning_thread_function,
3995:         this
3996:     );
3997:     if (!scanning_thread_) {
3998:         scanning_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
3999:     }
4000: }
4001: 
4002: 
4003: void ScanningCoordinator::stop_coordinated_scanning() {
4004:     //1. First check if thread is active at all
4005:     if (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
4006:         // 2. Reset flag. Thread will see this in while(scanning_active_) loop and exit.
4007:         scanning_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
4008: 
4009:         // 3. If thread pointer exists, wait for its completion.
4010:         if (scanning_thread_) {
4011:             // chThdWait blocks current (UI) thread until scanning_thread_ calls chThdExit
4012:             chThdWait(scanning_thread_);
4013:             scanning_thread_ = nullptr;
4014:         }
4015:     }
4016: }
4017: 
4018: msg_t ScanningCoordinator::scanning_thread_function(void* arg) {
4019:     return static_cast<ScanningCoordinator*>(arg)->coordinated_scanning_thread();
4020: }
4021: 
4022: msg_t ScanningCoordinator::coordinated_scanning_thread() {
4023:     while (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
4024:         scanner_.perform_scan_cycle(hardware_);
4025:         // TODO[CRITICAL][FIXED]: Removed direct UI calls from scanning thread
4026:         // UI updates now happen only through MessageHandler in handle_scanner_update()
4027: 
4028:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(scan_interval_ms_);
4029:     }
4030:     scanning_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
4031:     scanning_thread_ = nullptr;
4032:     chThdExit(0);
4033:     return 0;
4034: }
4035: 
4036: void ScanningCoordinator::update_runtime_parameters(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) {
4037:     scan_interval_ms_ = settings.scan_interval_ms;
4038: 
4039:     // Update scanner parameters if scanning is active
4040:     if (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
4041:         scanner_.update_scan_range(settings.wideband_min_freq_hz,
4042:                                    settings.wideband_max_freq_hz);
4043:     }
4044: }

4048: }

4056: void DroneDisplayController::get_max_power_for_current_bin(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum, uint8_t bin, uint8_t& max_power) {
4057:     if (bin >= spectrum.db.size()) {
4058:         max_power = 0;
4059:         return;
4060:     }
4061:     max_power = spectrum.db[bin];
4062: }
4063: 
4064: void DroneDisplayController::add_spectrum_pixel(uint8_t power) {
4065:     // ?? ФАЗА 1.5: Проверка валидности буфера (статический буфер)
4066:     if (!buffers_allocated_) {
4067:         return;
4068:     }
4069:     if (pixel_index < spectrum_row_buffer().size()) {
4070:         spectrum_row_buffer()[pixel_index] = spectrum_gradient_.lut[power];
4071:         pixel_index++;
4072:     }
4073: }

4075: 
4076: // ===========================================
4077: // PART 7: ENHANCED SETTINGS VALIDATOR
4078: // ===========================================
4079: 
4080: EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::ValidationResult
4081: EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_all(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) {
4082:     ValidationResult result;
4083: 
4084:     // 1. Validate RSSI threshold
4085:     if (!validate_rssi_threshold(settings.rssi_threshold_db, result.error_message, sizeof(result.error_message))) {
4086:         result.is_valid = false;
4087:         return result;
4088:     }
4089: 
4090:     // 2. Validate scan interval
4091:     if (!validate_scan_interval(settings.scan_interval_ms, result.error_message, sizeof(result.error_message))) {
4092:         result.is_valid = false;
4093:         return result;
4094:     }
4095: 
4096:     // 3. Validate audio parameters
4097:     if (!validate_audio_params(settings.audio_alert_frequency_hz,
4098:                               settings.audio_alert_duration_ms, result.error_message, sizeof(result.error_message))) {
4099:         result.is_valid = false;
4100:         return result;
4101:     }
4102: 
4103:     // 4. Validate bandwidth
4104:     if (!validate_bandwidth(settings.hardware_bandwidth_hz, result.error_message, sizeof(result.error_message))) {
4105:         result.is_valid = false;
4106:         return result;
4107:     }
4108: 
4109:     // 5. Validate frequency range
4110:     if (!validate_frequency_range(settings.user_min_freq_hz, settings.user_max_freq_hz, result.error_message, sizeof(result.error_message))) {
4111:         result.is_valid = false;
4112:         return result;
4113:     }
4114: 
4115:     // 6. Check for warnings (not errors)
4116:     if (settings.rssi_threshold_db > -60) {
4117:         result.warning_count++;
4118:         safe_strcat(result.error_message, "WARN: High RSSI threshold may miss weak signals\n", sizeof(result.error_message));
4119:     }
4120: 
4121:     if (settings.scan_interval_ms > 5000) {
4122:         result.warning_count++;
4123:         safe_strcat(result.error_message, "WARN: Slow scan interval\n", sizeof(result.error_message));
4124:     }
4125: 
4126:     return result;
4127: }
4128: 
4129: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_frequency(Frequency freq, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4130:     if (freq < DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ ||
4131:         freq > DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
4132:         char freq_str[32];
4133:         format_frequency_hz(freq, freq_str, sizeof(freq_str));
4134:         snprintf(error, error_size, "Frequency %s out of range (must be %llu-%llu GHz)",
4135:                  freq_str,
4136:                  DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ / 1000000000ULL,
4137:                  DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ / 1000000000ULL);
4138:         return false;
4139:     }
4140:     return true;
4141: }
4142: 
4143: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_rssi_threshold(int32_t rssi, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4144:     if (rssi < DroneConstants::MIN_VALID_RSSI || rssi > DroneConstants::MAX_VALID_RSSI) {
4145:         snprintf(error, error_size, "RSSI threshold %ld invalid (must be %ld to %ld)",
4146:                  (long)rssi, (long)DroneConstants::MIN_VALID_RSSI, (long)DroneConstants::MAX_VALID_RSSI);
4147:         return false;
4148:     }
4149:     return true;
4150: }
4151: 
4152: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_scan_interval(uint32_t interval_ms, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4153:     if (interval_ms < DroneConstants::MIN_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS ||
4154:         interval_ms > DroneConstants::MAX_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS) {
4155:         snprintf(error, error_size, "Scan interval %lu invalid (must be %lu to %lu)",
4156:                  (unsigned long)interval_ms, (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MIN_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS,
4157:                  (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MAX_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS);
4158:         return false;
4159:     }
4160:     return true;
4161: }
4162: 
4163: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_audio_params(uint32_t freq_hz, uint32_t duration_ms, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4164:     if (freq_hz < DroneConstants::MIN_AUDIO_FREQ || freq_hz > DroneConstants::MAX_AUDIO_FREQ) {
4165:         snprintf(error, error_size, "Audio frequency %lu invalid (must be %lu to %lu)",
4166:                  (unsigned long)freq_hz, (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MIN_AUDIO_FREQ,
4167:                  (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MAX_AUDIO_FREQ);
4168:         return false;
4169:     }
4170: 
4171:     if (duration_ms < DroneConstants::MIN_AUDIO_DURATION ||
4172:         duration_ms > DroneConstants::MAX_AUDIO_DURATION) {
4173:         snprintf(error, error_size, "Audio duration %lu invalid (must be %lu to %lu)",
4174:                  (unsigned long)duration_ms, (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MIN_AUDIO_DURATION,
4175:                  (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MAX_AUDIO_DURATION);
4176:         return false;
4177:     }
4178:     return true;
4179: }
4180: 
4181: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_bandwidth(uint32_t bandwidth_hz, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4182:     if (bandwidth_hz < DroneConstants::MIN_BANDWIDTH || bandwidth_hz > DroneConstants::MAX_BANDWIDTH) {
4183:         snprintf(error, error_size, "Bandwidth %lu invalid (must be %lu to %lu)",
4184:                  (unsigned long)bandwidth_hz, (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MIN_BANDWIDTH,
4185:                  (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MAX_BANDWIDTH);
4186:         return false;
4187:     }
4188:     return true;
4189: }
4190: 
4191: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_frequency_range(Frequency min_hz, Frequency max_hz, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4192:     if (min_hz >= max_hz) {
4193:         safe_strcpy(error, "Min frequency must be less than max frequency", error_size);
4194:         return false;
4195:     }
4196: 
4197:     if (!validate_frequency(min_hz, error, error_size)) return false;
4198:     if (!validate_frequency(max_hz, error, error_size)) return false;
4199: 
4200:     // Check range width
4201:     Frequency range = max_hz - min_hz;
4202:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(range) < 1000000ULL) { // Minimum 1 MHz range
4203:         safe_strcpy(error, "Frequency range too small (minimum 1 MHz)", error_size);
4204:         return false;
4205:     }
4206:     
4207:     return true;
4208: }
4209: 
4210: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::is_known_drone_band(Frequency freq) {
4211:     // Check 433 MHz band
4212:     if (freq >= DroneConstants::MIN_433MHZ && freq <= DroneConstants::MAX_433MHZ) return true;
4213:     
4214:     // Check 860-930 MHz (LRS/Military)
4215:     if (freq >= DroneConstants::MIN_900MHZ && freq <= DroneConstants::MAX_900MHZ) return true;
4216:     
4217:     // Check 2.4 GHz ISM band
4218:     if (freq >= DroneConstants::MIN_24GHZ && freq <= DroneConstants::MAX_24GHZ) return true;
4219:     
4220:     // Check 5.8 GHz band
4221:     if (freq >= DroneConstants::MIN_58GHZ && freq <= DroneConstants::MAX_58GHZ) return true;
4222:     
4223:     return false;
4224: }
4225: 
4226: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::is_ism_band(Frequency freq) {
4227:     return (static_cast<uint64_t>(freq) >= 2400000000ULL && static_cast<uint64_t>(freq) <= 2483500000ULL) ||
4228:            (static_cast<uint64_t>(freq) >= 5725000000ULL && static_cast<uint64_t>(freq) <= 5875000000ULL);
4229: }

4232: // Eliminates ~30 lines of duplicate formatting code

4234: void EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::format_frequency_hz(Frequency freq, char* buffer, size_t buffer_size) {
4235:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(freq) >= 1000000000ULL) {
4236:         FrequencyFormatter::format_to_buffer(buffer, buffer_size, freq, FrequencyFormatter::Format::DETAILED_GHZ);
4237:     } else {
4238:         FrequencyFormatter::format_to_buffer(buffer, buffer_size, freq, FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ);
4239:     }
4240: }

4284: void CompactFrequencyRuler::paint(Painter& painter) {
4285:     const auto r = screen_rect();
4286:

4288:

4290:

4293: 
4294: void CompactFrequencyRuler::draw_compact_ticks(Painter& painter, const Rect r) {
4295:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4296:     if (range == 0) return;  // Early exit pattern
4297: 
4298:     Frequency tick_interval = calculate_optimal_tick_interval();
4299:     if (tick_interval == 0) return;
4300: 
4301:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Single style (both use same font/colors)
4302:     // Eliminates branching between mhz/ghz styles
4303:     static Style label_style{font::fixed_5x8, Color::grey(), Color::black()};
4304: 
4305:     // Draw horizontal line at bottom of ruler (using 1-pixel rectangle)
4306:     painter.fill_rectangle(
4307:         {r.left(), r.top() + RULER_HEIGHT - 1, r.width(), 1},
4308:         Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4309:     );
4310: 
4311:     Frequency first_tick = (min_freq_ / tick_interval) * tick_interval;
4312:     if (first_tick < min_freq_) {
4313:         first_tick += tick_interval;
4314:     }
4315: 
4316:     for (Frequency tick = first_tick; tick <= max_freq_; tick += tick_interval) {
4317:         int x = r.left() + static_cast<int>(((tick - min_freq_) * spectrum_width_) / range);
4318: 
4319:         if (x < r.left() || x > r.right()) {
4320:             continue;
4321:         }
4322: 
4323:         // Draw major tick (tall) - using 1-pixel rectangle
4324:         painter.fill_rectangle(
4325:             {x, r.top(), 1, TICK_HEIGHT_MAJOR},
4326:             Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4327:         );
4328: 
4329:         std::string label = format_compact_label(tick);
4330: 
4331:         auto text_size = label_style.font.size_of(label);
4332:         int text_x = x - text_size.width() / 2;
4333:         int text_y = r.top() + 1;
4334: 
4335:         if (text_x < r.left() + 2) text_x = r.left() + 2;
4336:         if (text_x + text_size.width() > r.right() - 2) {
4337:             text_x = r.right() - text_size.width() - 2;
4338:         }
4339: 
4340:         painter.draw_string({text_x, text_y}, label_style, label);
4341: 
4342:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Sub-tick logic based on tick_interval only
4343:         // Eliminates should_use_mhz() call (bitfield read cost)
4344:         if (static_cast<uint64_t>(tick_interval) >= 100000000ULL) {
4345:             for (int sub = 1; sub < 5; sub++) {
4346:                 Frequency sub_tick = tick + (tick_interval * sub) / 5;
4347:                 int sub_x = r.left() + static_cast<int>(((sub_tick - min_freq_) * spectrum_width_) / range);
4348: 
4349:                 if (sub_x > r.left() && sub_x < r.right()) {
4350:                     painter.fill_rectangle(
4351:                         {sub_x, r.top(), 1, TICK_HEIGHT_MINOR},
4352:                         Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4353:                     );
4354:                 }
4355:             }
4356:         }
4357:     }
4358: }
4359: 
4360: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Lookup table for ruler style to formatter mapping
4361: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
4362: // Eliminates ~60 lines of switch-case logic
4363: namespace {
4364:     static constexpr FrequencyFormatter::Format RULER_FORMAT_LUT[] = {
4365:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::COMPACT_GHZ,   // COMPACT_GHZ = 0
4366:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::COMPACT_MHZ,   // COMPACT_MHZ = 1
4367:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_GHZ,  // STANDARD_GHZ = 2
4368:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ,  // STANDARD_MHZ = 3
4369:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::DETAILED_GHZ,  // DETAILED = 4
4370:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::SPACED_GHZ      // SPACED_GHZ = 5
4371:     };
4372: }
4373: 
4374: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified frequency formatting using FrequencyFormatter
4375: // Eliminates ~60 lines of duplicate formatting code
4376: // Scott Meyers Item 2: Prefer consts, enums, and inlines to #defines
4377: std::string CompactFrequencyRuler::format_compact_label(Frequency freq) {
4378:     // LUT lookup instead of switch-case (Flash storage, zero RAM allocation)
4379:     uint8_t idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(ruler_style_);
4380:     if (idx >= 6) idx = 0;  // Fallback to COMPACT_GHZ
4381:     
4382:     return FrequencyFormatter::format(freq, RULER_FORMAT_LUT[idx]);
4383: }
4384: 
4385: Frequency CompactFrequencyRuler::calculate_optimal_tick_interval() {
4386:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4387:     if (range == 0) return 0;
4388: 
4389:     // Optimized intervals for PortaPack's small screen
4390:     // Prioritize GHz intervals for SPACED_GHZ style
4391:     Frequency intervals[] = {
4392:         5000000000ULL,  4000000000ULL,  3000000000ULL, 2000000000ULL,  // 5G, 4G, 3G, 2G
4393:         1000000000ULL,  // 1G (key for SPACED_GHZ)
4394:         500000000ULL,   250000000ULL,   200000000ULL,            // 500M, 250M, 200M
4395:         100000000ULL,   50000000ULL,    25000000ULL,            // 100M, 50M, 25M
4396:         20000000ULL,    10000000ULL,    5000000ULL,             // 20M, 10M, 5M
4397:         2000000ULL,     1000000ULL,     500000ULL,              // 2M, 1M, 500k
4398:         200000ULL,      100000ULL                                // 200k, 100k
4399:     };
4400: 
4401:     for (auto interval : intervals) {
4402:         int ticks = static_cast<int>(range / interval);
4403:         if (ticks >= target_tick_count_ - 1 && ticks <= target_tick_count_ + 1) {
4404:             return interval;
4405:         }
4406:     }
4407: 
4408:     return range / target_tick_count_;
4409: }
4410: 
4411: RulerStyle CompactFrequencyRuler::determine_auto_style() {
4412:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4413:     bool use_mhz = should_use_mhz_labels();
4414: 
4415:     if (use_mhz) {
4416:         if (static_cast<uint64_t>(range) < 100000000ULL) {
4417:             return RulerStyle::DETAILED;
4418:         } else {
4419:             return RulerStyle::STANDARD_MHZ;
4420:         }
4421:     } else {
4422:         // Optimal for PortaPack: Use SPACED_GHZ for wide ranges (>1GHz)
4423:         if (static_cast<uint64_t>(range) >= 1000000000ULL) {
4424:             return RulerStyle::SPACED_GHZ;
4425:         } else if (static_cast<uint64_t>(range) >= 500000000ULL) {
4426:             return RulerStyle::STANDARD_GHZ;
4427:         } else {
4428:             return RulerStyle::COMPACT_GHZ;
4429:         }
4430:     }
4431: }
4432: 
4433: bool CompactFrequencyRuler::should_use_mhz_labels() const {
4434:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4435: 
4436:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(range) < 50000000ULL) {
4437:         return true;
4438:     }
4439: 
4440:     Frequency center = (min_freq_ + max_freq_) / 2;
4441:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(center) < 1000000000ULL) {
4442:         return true;
4443:     }
4444: 
4445:     if (ruler_style_ == RulerStyle::COMPACT_MHZ ||
4446:         ruler_style_ == RulerStyle::STANDARD_MHZ) {
4447:         return true;
4448:     }
4449: 
4450:     return false;
4451: }

4481:         hidden(false);

4484: 
4485: Frequency FrequencyRuler::calculate_tick_interval() {
4486:     Frequency freq_range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4487:     if (freq_range == 0) {
4488:         return 1000000000ULL;  // Default: 1 GHz
4489:     }
4490: 
4491:     // Possible intervals in Hz (from largest to smallest)
4492:     Frequency intervals[] = {
4493:         4000000000ULL,  // 4 GHz
4494:         2000000000ULL,  // 2 GHz
4495:         1000000000ULL,  // 1 GHz
4496:         500000000ULL,   // 500 MHz
4497:         200000000ULL,   // 200 MHz
4498:         100000000ULL,   // 100 MHz
4499:         50000000ULL,    // 50 MHz
4500:         20000000ULL,    // 20 MHz
4501:         10000000ULL,    // 10 MHz
4502:         5000000ULL,     // 5 MHz
4503:         2000000ULL,     // 2 MHz
4504:         1000000ULL      // 1 MHz
4505:     };
4506: 
4507:     size_t num_intervals = sizeof(intervals) / sizeof(intervals[0]);
4508: 
4509:     // Select interval so that we have 4-8 ticks on screen
4510:     for (size_t i = 0; i < num_intervals; i++) {
4511:         if (freq_range / intervals[i] <= 8 && freq_range / intervals[i] >= 4) {
4512:             return intervals[i];
4513:         }
4514:     }
4515: 
4516:     // Fallback: use 6 ticks evenly distributed
4517:     return freq_range / 6;
4518: }
4519: 
4520: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Lookup tables for frequency ruler configuration
4521: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
4522: // Eliminates conditional std::string allocation and branching
4523: namespace {
4524:     // Tick configuration LUT (Flash storage, zero RAM at runtime)
4525:     struct TickConfig {
4526:         FrequencyFormatter::Format format;
4527:         uint8_t sub_ticks;  // Bitfield: 0=none, 1..5=count
4528:     };
4529: 
4530:     static constexpr TickConfig TICK_CONFIG_LUT[] = {
4531:         {FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_GHZ, 5},  // >= 1 GHz
4532:         {FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ, 5},  // >= 1 MHz
4533:         {FrequencyFormatter::Format::COMPACT_MHZ, 0}    // < 1 MHz
4534:     };
4535: 
4536:     // Get config index from tick_interval (constexpr-friendly)
4537:     constexpr uint8_t get_tick_config_index(Frequency tick_interval) {
4538:         return (static_cast<uint64_t>(tick_interval) >= 1000000000ULL) ? 0 :
4539:                (static_cast<uint64_t>(tick_interval) >= 1000000ULL) ? 1 : 2;
4540:     }
4541: }
4542: 
4543: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified frequency formatting using FrequencyFormatter
4544: // Eliminates ~40 lines of duplicate formatting code
4545: std::string FrequencyRuler::format_frequency_label(Frequency freq, Frequency tick_interval) {
4546:     // LUT lookup instead of conditional (Flash string, zero RAM allocation)
4547:     uint8_t idx = get_tick_config_index(tick_interval);
4548:     return FrequencyFormatter::format(freq, TICK_CONFIG_LUT[idx].format);
4549: }
4550: 
4551: void FrequencyRuler::draw_frequency_ticks(Painter& painter, const Rect r) {
4552:     Frequency tick_interval = calculate_tick_interval();
4553:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4554:     if (range == 0) return;  // Early exit pattern
4555: 
4556:     // LUT lookup for configuration (Flash storage, zero RAM allocation)
4557:     const TickConfig& config = TICK_CONFIG_LUT[get_tick_config_index(tick_interval)];
4558: 
4559:     // Style for tick labels (small font 5x8)
4560:     static Style ruler_style{font::fixed_5x8, Color::grey(), Color::black()};
4561: 
4562:     // Draw horizontal line at bottom of ruler (using 1-pixel rectangle)
4563:     painter.fill_rectangle(
4564:         {r.left(), r.top() + RULER_HEIGHT - 1, r.width(), 1},
4565:         Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4566:     );
4567: 
4568:     // Find first tick
4569:     Frequency first_tick = (min_freq_ / tick_interval) * tick_interval;
4570:     if (first_tick < min_freq_) {
4571:         first_tick += tick_interval;
4572:     }
4573: 
4574:     // Draw ticks and labels
4575:     for (Frequency tick = first_tick; tick <= max_freq_; tick += tick_interval) {
4576:         // Convert frequency to x position
4577:         int x = r.left() + static_cast<int>(((tick - min_freq_) * spectrum_width_) / range);
4578: 
4579:         if (x < r.left() || x > r.right()) {
4580:             continue;
4581:         }
4582: 
4583:         // Draw major tick (tall) - using 1-pixel rectangle
4584:         painter.fill_rectangle(
4585:             {x, r.top(), 1, TICK_HEIGHT_MAJOR},
4586:             Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4587:         );
4588: 
4589:         // Format and draw text label (LUT lookup, no std::string allocation for unit)
4590:         std::string label = format_frequency_label(tick, tick_interval);
4591: 
4592:         auto text_size = ruler_style.font.size_of(label);
4593:         int text_x = x - text_size.width() / 2;
4594:         int text_y = r.top() + 1;
4595: 
4596:         // Clamp text position to screen bounds
4597:         if (text_x < r.left() + 2) text_x = r.left() + 2;
4598:         if (text_x + text_size.width() > r.right() - 2) {
4599:             text_x = r.right() - text_size.width() - 2;
4600:         }
4601: 
4602:         painter.draw_string({text_x, text_y}, ruler_style, label);
4603: 
4604:         // Add intermediate ticks if configured (LUT lookup, zero branching)
4605:         for (uint8_t sub = 1; sub <= config.sub_ticks; sub++) {
4606:             Frequency sub_tick = tick + (tick_interval * sub) / (config.sub_ticks + 1);
4607:             int sub_x = r.left() + static_cast<int>(((sub_tick - min_freq_) * spectrum_width_) / range);
4608: 
4609:             if (sub_x > r.left() && sub_x < r.right()) {
4610:                 painter.fill_rectangle(
4611:                     {sub_x, r.top(), 1, TICK_HEIGHT_MINOR},
4612:                     Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4613:                 );
4614:             }
4615:         }
4616:     }
4617: }
4618: 
4619: void FrequencyRuler::paint(Painter& painter) {
4620:     const auto r = screen_rect();
4621: 
4622:     // Fill background
4623:     painter.fill_rectangle(r, Color::black());
4624: 
4625:     // Draw frequency ticks and labels
4626:     if (visible_) {
4627:         draw_frequency_ticks(painter, r);
4628:     }
4629: }

4640:     frequency_ruler_.set_visible(false);
4641: }
4642: 
4643: void DroneDisplayController::apply_display_settings(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) {
4644:     if (settings.display_flags.show_frequency_ruler) {
4645:         compact_frequency_ruler_.set_visible(true);
4646:         frequency_ruler_.set_visible(false);
4647: 
4648:         if (settings.display_flags.auto_ruler_style) {
4649:             compact_frequency_ruler_.set_ruler_style(RulerStyle::COMPACT_GHZ);
4650:         } else {
4651:             // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT в Flash вместо switch (строки 4135-4144)
4652:             uint8_t style_idx = (settings.frequency_ruler_style < 7) ?
4653:                                 settings.frequency_ruler_style : 0;
4654:             compact_frequency_ruler_.set_ruler_style(RULER_STYLE_LUT[style_idx]);
4655:         }
4656: 
4657:         compact_frequency_ruler_.set_tick_count(settings.compact_ruler_tick_count);
4658:     } else {
4659:         compact_frequency_ruler_.set_visible(false);
4660:         frequency_ruler_.set_visible(false);
4661:     }
4662: }
